KUYICALA UKUFOTHOKHOPHA NOMA YILIPHI IKHASI KULE NCWADI NGAPHANDLE KWEMVUME EBHALWE   
AMAZWIBELA OMLOBI 
Ngithi ake ngithathe leli thuba lokuba ngiphose itshe esivivaneni somlando wenhlanhla. Mhlasimbe nami ngingahle ngihlomule kuleyo nqatho yenqobe yokugcina yonyaka. Bakwethu uma ingane isabhibhidla, akuze kungalindeleka ukuba ihlafune umtharno omkhulu ongahlafunwa ngumuntu osenamazinyo aphelele. Nami kulesi sivivane engiphosa kuso itshe engithi yisivivane senhlanhla, yitshe nje elingatheni, engingasho futhi ngithi kule nqatho engizarna ukuhlomula kuyo ingeyenqobe ngempela, ngamagqalingana nje angasho lutho. 
  Ngalokhu bakwethu ngizama ukuxolisa kinina ngamaphutha eniyothuka nihlangana nawo. Kuyisicelo sami ukuba niwabekezelele. Nicabange nje ukuthi enziwe yimfundamakhwela, evukwe wusinga, namadlingozi yase igiya. Igiya njalo kayiphethe narndlelo naqhabanga lokugiya. Nokuncwada kayincwadile. Kanti nobuxhwe futhi bumagange. Ngakho uma nibona ngiphambana nehlombe kuyobe kufakazela lezi zizathu esengizibale ngenhla ... 
  Lapha ekuchithekeni koPhoko lokuqala kuze kuyofinyelela kolwesibili olusamumethwe, ngizame ukwakha uxhaxha lohlaka lwamatharnbo, engethemba ukuthi ayoba wusizo kulabo abayokwazi ukufaka inyama. Ikakhulukazi labo ebebephokophele ukwazi ngemvelaphi yabo. Ngokuloba leli bhukwana nelizolandela ngizama khona ukwelekelela labo abebezihlupha ngalokhu. 
  Lapha-ke ngiqale ngenkinga yokuthi izizwe ezakhele leli likaMthaniya zehlukene kangakanani. Nokuthi ulimi lwesiZulu lukhulunywa kanjani isifunda ngesifunda. Kanti ngizame nokuveza ukuthi izibongo zavela kanjani. Okokuqala zikhona ezavela ngamagama abantu. Zikhona ezavela ngezigemegeme ezavelela leso sigejana esithize sabantu. Kanti ezinye izibongo zivela ngesenzo esithile somuntu othize, bese kuthi inzalo yakhe ibizwe ngaleso senzo. 
 
  Ngiyethemba Mabandla kaMjokwane kaNdaba ukuthi lapha bengibhekene nengwadla uqobo ekuhla2;iyeni izibongo zabantu, isibongo ngesibongo. Kulo leli bhuku ngizame ukuchaza umehluko phakathi kwesibongo nesithakazelo kanye nesithopho. Ngokwethula leli bhuku kinina eliyimizamo yami yokuqala yokugubha' nokuphenya ngemvelaphi kanye nendabuko yabantu, ngikuthatha njengokubhibhidla uqobo. Angiphinde ngithi bandla lakwethu ningixolele lapho nihlangana khona namaphutha. Okwenu nje okukhulu ukuba nihlafune lokho enikutholayo, nikugwinye kunjalo. Noma nicofiya izimpepha zalo mgqakazo ophekwe ungeliwe, wasefwa, kodwa zamani ukucolisa. Ngiyanethembisa ukuthi njengoba kuseligalelo lokuqala leli, inkonyane isethuka isisinga, ngokuzayo niyothola ifutho langempela, hhayi inqobe. Manje ake ngithathe leli thuba lokuthokoza kwami, ngikubhekise kubantu ababeka isoyi ukuze Ie ndlu yakheke. Owokuqala engizodlulisa ukuthokoza kwami kuye nguzakwethu ngokomsebenzi laphaya oKhozini (Radio Zulu) ngaphansi kwenhlangano yokusakaza (SABC). Lowo ngumfokaNzimande uB.W. Nzimande. 
  Wangikhuthaza kakhulu ukuba ngilobe lokhu esengikulobile manje. Waze wadela isikhathi sakhe wasinika mina engikhombisa ukuthi abantu bayifuna kabi imvelaphi yabo. Lokho kwanginika olukhulu ugqozi. Ngithi Mphephethwa, unwele oludel Ngiyethemba usuyazibona izithelo zenkuthazo yakho. Ukhombisile ukuthi uma ubona ithalente kumuntu awuliyeki licwile, kodwa uzama ngayo yonke indleia ukuthi lihlale obala libonwe ngabantu. Angiphinde ngithi unwele olude Mfowethul 
  Owesibili engimbongayo yinkosazana kaNginikeza eyisandla sami sokuphonsa, ngoba ibihlala nami ubusuku bonke uma sengithanda ukudembesela kodwa ibe yiphela endlebeni ithi mangiqhubeke. Kuwena Nonkosi ngithi nje isisho esithi ' "Lapho kukhona khona indoda ephumelelayo, kukhona owesifazane ohlakaniphile emva kwakhe.' Ngithi Shwabadal MthiyaneJ 
  Owesithathu ofanele ukubongwa nokutuswa, yintombi kaT?endelana kaNyosana, kaMadwala, kaSoshingose. Intombi ~nglzalayo, okwakuthi uma inqola isijamile ngolwazi. Iqhamuke yona ithi chabo lapha kwenziwa kanje. Nami bese ??enza lokhu engitshele khona. Nempela ngiyoyibona inqola lSlhamba: futhi isisitheka ulwazi olunzulu. Ngithi kuwena; Mana njalo Ndina kaMnisii Wena waseMvulenil Lenyise kwenela Ithole lakho, noma belimunya limi ngezinyawo. 
  !<ukhon.a futhi abanye ebebengikhuthaza ukuba ngithathe uSlba ngliobe. Ngakuvuma lokhu ngazi kahle ukuthi ngiyimf.undamakhwela kulo mkhakha. Ngakho kufanele ngedlulise ukubonga kwami okukhulu ngikubhekise kumuntu owaba ngmnzanyana wale ngane okungathi izalwe kungakabi isikha.thi. Lowo nguMnu. L.Z.M. Khumalo. Ngithi wena kaMajubane amabili, elokuya nelokubuya, wena weMbindla emashobashobal Wena weNdlondlol Angibongi ngiyanconcoz~, n?oba nguwena okuthe uma sengigajwe yilo mse~enzl, ngljlyelw.e ukuthi ngiwenze njani. kodwa ngabuye ngazlduduza ngokuthi ukhona wena. Lo msebenzi ngiyowethula kuwena uwusingathe ngowakwenu. 
  Bese ngithi emabandleni kaMjokwane kaNdaba, nina ?a.k~Ph~nga noMageba klezani nani kule mazi engunondlini, ihmlkaZ! uqobo, eniyethulelwa ngokaMashobana, kaDonda kangakanani, nasentendeni yesandla uyenela, kaMbuzi zizele zonke kodwa zibe zingenampongo. Size sihlangane esigabeni esilandelayo.

INqABE ABANTV ABAKHELE .ISIFVNDAZWE SASENATALI BAVELAPHI? 
Abantu abakhele izwekazi laseNatali elingaphansi koMzansi ne-Afrika kuthiwa nabo badabuka eNkabazwe njengazo zonke izizwe ezisenWa nezwe lase-Afrika. 
Ukusuka kwabantu abamnyama behla nezwe, kuthiwa 
babehlukene izigaba ezimbili ezinkulu okwakungabeSuthu . kanye nabeNguni. KubeSuthu sikhuluma ngabaPedi, abeTswana kanye. nabeSuthu bakaMshweshwe. Kanti uma sikhuluma ngabeNguni, sikhuluma ngamaSwazi, amaZulu, kanye namaXhosa. AbeSuthu bonke bahlanganiswa ukukhuluma kwabo, kanti futhi bacishe batholakale endaweni noma esifundeni esisodwa noma ezifundeni ezakhelene, njengoba sibathola abeSuthu abangabaPedi eNyakatho kuyela eMpumalanga neNtilasifali, kanti abeTswana bona batholakala ikakhulukazi ngaseNtshonalanga yeNtilasifali kanye nasecl:iosheni laseKoloni (Northern Cape). Kanti abeSuthu bakaMshweshwe bona batholakala eFulesitata kanye naseLusuthu kuze kuyofika kwelaMahiligwa (Griqualand). 
  Isizwe samaNguni sona sitholakala KwaNgwalle (eSwazini), KwaZulu kanye naKwaXhosa kwelaseKoloni; ikakhulukazi eMpumalanga nalo. Njengoba sithi abeNguni beWukene lezi zigaba futhi sasho ukuthi basuka enhla nezwe, babehamba behlukana izigatshana eziningana ezenza ukuba abeNguni behlukahlukane, ikakhulukazi uma bekhuluma ukuthi nhloboni yoMnguni lona nokuthi uvela kusiphi isifunda ngoba

  Okokuqala ake siqale futhi siwahlahlele siwakhiphe izitho zawo ukuze kube lula ukuqonda esikhuluma ngakho. Nokuthi siwulandele umsuka wendabuko yesibongo ngesibongo.   Ngingalinganisa nje ngezibongo ezidurnile esizaziyo lapha kulesi sifunda sakithi ezaqala ngamagama kwagdna sekuyizibongo. EsakwaQwabe, savela ngendodana kaMalandela endala uQwabe, kanti esakwaZulu, sasivela ngendodana encane kaMalandela uZulu. Kanti esakwaNtombela savela ngoNtombela indodana kaLuzumane. Laphake kulezi zibongo kungenzeka kube nengozi yokuthi ngenxa yokufana kwamagama okhokho bese kwenzeka ukuthi kube khona izibongo okwethukeka zitholakale sezifana, kanti kazihIobene nakancane. Kukhona oGumede kaManukuza indodana kaMthonga kanti kukhona oGumede kaQwabe indodana kaMalandela abangahlobene nalaba bakaManukuza.

Kanti futhi oGumede bakaManukuza behlukene noGumede kaQwabe ngokuthi bona bangabeNguni abavela Embo kanti laba abanye bona bangaMantungwa. 
  Ezinye izibongo zidabuka ezenzweni ezithize, noma emikhutshaneni ethize. Ake sibheke nje ukuvela kwesibongo sakwaMkhize, kwakuthiwa ngabantu bemikhizo ngoba bethanda ukuhIala endaweni lapho likhiza khona yikho baze batholakala bezinze laphaya eQhudeni. Babethanda izindawo lapho likhiza khona ngoba kungabantu abafuye kakhulu izinkomo.

  Bonke babengamaNguni amasiko nezinjongo zabo zifana kuba khona lokho kushayisana kwezibongo. Sizokhumbula futhi ukuthi ukuqambeka kwamagama abantu kunencazelo ethize kanye nenjongo nesifiso esithize abazali balowo abasuke besifisa ngaye lowo muntu abasuke bemqamba. 
  Yingakho nje uzothola izingane zonke zabeNguni zinamagama afanayo ngoba anencazelo eyodwa nomlayezo owodwa ozwakalayo kulowo nalowo muntu onguMnguni. NakubeSuthu kunjalo. Uzothola ukuthi amagama abantu bakhona nawo ayafana noma anokufana okuthize ngoba ngokolimi Iwabo anencazelo ezwakalayo kubo.

Singabehlukanisa izigaba ezinhlanu. 
Isigaba sokuqala: AbaNguni baseMbo (EMbo Nguni) Lesi yisigaba esikhulu kunazo zonke ngoba simbandakanya zonke izibongo eziseSwazini kanye nezinye izibongo eziseNatali nakwaZulu. 
  Uma kulandelwa umlando nemvelaphi yalezi zibongo uthola ukuthi zihlobene futhi zidabuka ndawonye. Ezinye uthole ukuthi zinokhokho nomsunguli wazo oyedwa noma abantu 
	abahlobene 	ngokuzalana. Kuvamise ukuthi 	abantu 
	abangabaMbo 	ngabakwaMkhize bakaMumbo. 	Yebo 
singavuma, kodwa sithola bona laba abakwaMkhize ukuthi bavela kuMaNguni amakhulu akwaNgwane. Lokhu sokuchaza kahle uma sesixoxa ngezibongo uqobo. 
  Okungumahluko kubantu abangaseMbo ukuthi uma bekhuluma iningi labo Iithambisa ulimi lutekele noma sithi bayatekela lokhu sikubona noma sikuzwa kakhulu kumaSwazi. nakwezinye izizwe ezakhelene nawo kanjalo namaBhaca ngoba sithola ukuthi abanye abantu abangamaBhaca basuka khona kwaNgwane ngenxa yezimpi. Kukhona abanye abaseMbo asebagwinywa ngaMantungwa asebekhuluma isiNtungwa kakhulu kunesiMbo. Okungeke. usezwa ukuthi laba bantu banawo yini umehluko kumaNtungwa. Sizoziveza-ke zonke izibongo ezingaphansi kwalesi sigaba esengisichazile ngenhla.

Isigaba sesibili: AbaNguni baseBuThonga (AmaThonga Nguni) 
Lesi sigaba kasisikhulu kakhulu, ngoba ukuvela kwaso sengathi singumxhantela walesi sigaba esingenhla. Kodwa ngenlfa yokuthi laba bantu behlukana bathi ukuqhelelana ngezifunda zabo, ngokwakhelana nezinye izizwe ulimi lwabo lwaya ngokuya lushintsha kwadaleka olunye uhlobo oselwendkile kusiMbo Nguni, kodwa kuthande ukungena nesiShangane lapho . 
. , Laba bantu sibathola ngale kwezintaba zoBombo, endaweni yakwaMhlabuyalingana, kuthiwa yindawo. yaseButhonga. Izibongo esizithola lapha ngabakwaNgwane bakaZikhali (KwaMbila). AbakwaNxumalo kaPhumphele (KaMabaso), kwaJobe, kwaGumede kaSiqakatha, kwaGumede wakwaMduku, oTembe, oNgubane kanye nezinye izibongo eziyimixhantela.

  Kukhona engithanda ukukuchaza futhi' ngibona kuzoba wusizo olukhulu ekuhlaziyeni izibongo ngokwehlukana kwazo. Vma sikhulurna ngesizwe sisuke siqondeni, nalapho sikhuluma ngomndeni, okuyisibongo kanye nesigaba okuyisithakazelo bese sikhulurna ngesigejana okuyizithopho. Ake sikuhlaziye-ke nalokhu ngapharnbi kokuba siqhubeke nezibongo. 
ISIKHANYISO NGAMAGAMA ATHIZE 
Isizwe 
Vma sikhuluma ngeSizwe siqonde labo bantu abaqoqeke ndawonye ezweni elilodwa ngaphansi kombuso owodwa, kungenzeka ukuthi laba bantu kabakhulurni ulirni olulodwa kodwa ngenxa yokuthi bahIala ezweni elilodwa bakha isizwe. VShaka wahIanganisa izizwana eziningi wabumba isizwe esisodwa samaZulu. Lezi zizwana zaba yisizwe esisodwa ngaphansi kombuso owodwa waKwaZulu ngaphansi kwenkosi eyodwa. 
. Isibongo 
Ngesibongo sikhulurna ngornndeni othize ozihIanganise ngaphansi kukakhokho noma umholi wawo. Lowo rnndeni uye uzibize ngegama lalowo ongumsuka wawo. Kuharnba kuhambe Iowo mndeni uma usuwande kakhulu ube usuzibiza ngaleli gama kuze kube yisibongo ozokwaziwa ngaso. Yingakho nje sinesibongo sakwaZulu esivela kuZulu. VZulu kwakuyigama lomuntu. Abantwana bakhe baziwa ngokuthi abakwaZulu. 
Isithakazelo . 
Vma sikhuluma ngesithakazelo sikhuluma ngento esemqoka kakhulu kubantu abaNsundu ngoba uma umuntu waKwaZulu 
8 
umthakazele wenze into enkulu empilweni yakhe yonke. 
Kanti yini isithakazelo? Sehluke ngani futhi esibongweni? 
Irnpendulo kayilula ngoba kukhona abathatha isithakazelo basenze isibongo abanye bathathe isibongo basenze isithakazelo. Empeleni ungeke ubasole abenze njalo ngoba ukuvela kwesithakazelo kanye nesibongo kakunawo umehluko omkhulu, ngoba nizokhumbula ukuthi isithakazelo sivela egameni lomuntu oylnhIoko yalowo rnndeni owela ngaphansi kwaleso sibongo. Vmehluko omkhulu phakathi kwesibongo nesithakazelo ngokubona kwami, wukuthi isithakazelo siba ngesabantu bezibongo eziningi ezahIukene kodwa zibe zidabuka enhlokweni eyodwa yornndeni. 
  Isibongo sivela enhlokweni yornndeni kwehle ngoliba lwaso, kodwa isithakazelo sithinta abantwana benhloko yornndeni eyasungula leso sibongo, noma okwasungulwa leso sibongo kususelwa kuyo kwase kudaleka izibongo eziningi ezixhantele kulesi sibongo esikhulu. 
  Ake ngilinganise ngesibongo sakwaKhumalo, Mabaso, Nkosi (Ndlangamandla), izibongo Iezi ezehlukene ngokubona kwabantu. Futhi narni ngisho njalo ngoba zinamagama ehlukile futhi zizirnele kasikho esendke kwesinye, kodwa kukhona into ebalulekile okuyiyona ezihlanganisayo Iezi zibongo. 
  Vma uhIangana nomuntu ukuthi kuyena Mntungwa nakuMabaso noNkosi. 
Ngubani 10 Mntungwa futhi ngubani 10 Mbulazi? 
UMntungwa nguyise kaMabaso noKhumalo. Ungukhokho kaSiwela ozaia abakwaNkosi. UMbulazi nguyise kaMntungwa uyise woKhumalo noMabaso. 
  Uma usubheka lokhu kulinganisa engikwenze ngenhla ngalezi zibongo ezehIukene, kukhomba ukuthi kukhona okuzihIanganisayo. Le nto ezihlanganisayo ethi Mntungwa kaMbulazi, iyisithakazelo. Ngakho Ie nto ehlanganisa izibongo ezirlingi ezahlukahIukene yenza umuntu abone ukuthi noma zahlukene nje lezi zibongo kodwa zivela ndawonye, umsuka 
, 
wazo munye. 

  
Isithopho 
Ngenye yezinto ebadidayo abantu lena, Iningi kalikwazi ukwehlukanisa isithopho kanye nesithakazelo. Emndenini owodwa onesithakazelo esisodwa. kuba khona ukwahlukahlukana kwezindlu. Nginikhumbuze nje ukuthi emndenini owodwa wendoda eyodwa kuba khona izindlu ezahlukahlukene ngobukhulu bazo. 
  Kuba khona Indlunkulu lapho kuphuma khona inkosana. bese kuba khona iKhohlwa eliba ngunkosikazi wesibili. bese kuba khona iQadi okungunkosikazi wesithathu emzini wendoda. Uma indoda isaqhubeka nokuganwa kuba khona neSokanqangi okungunkosikazi wesine ongeniswa eKhohlweni kanti iQadi lona lingeniswa eNdiunkulu. Angiqondile lapha ukuchaza ngezindlu kodwa ngiqonde ukukhuluma ngesithopho noma ngezithopho kanye nokuvela kwazo. Ke ngibuye ngilinganise ngoKhumalo noMabaso. Lana ngamadodana endoda eyodwa kodwa base bakha imindeni eyahlukene. kwakhona owakwaKhumalo osekuyisibongo manje sakwaKhumalo. bese kuba khona ngokunjalo owakwaMabaso nawo futhi sekuyisibongo. 
  Noma lezi zibongo zivela ndawonye kepha ngeke usho ukuthi kumuntu wakwaMabaso. Mashobana noma Mzilikazi kaMashobana ngoba akumthinti yena ngoba laba ngabendlu kaKhumalo hhayi ekaMabaso. kayithinteki. Ngokunjalo ngeke usho kumuntu wakwaKhumalo ukuthi wena kaGqikazi. ngoba akumthinti yena kodwa kuthinta indlu kaMabaso. 
  Ngakho uma uthopha umuntu umthopha ngoyise noma ngoyisemkhulu. Umuntu wakwaZulu angakukhiphela noma yini engale uma nje umthophile. Ungambiza ngesibongo sakhe. umthakazele. kodwa ngeke kufane nokuba umthophile. Lapho usuke uthinte inhliziyo yakhe ekhoneni. ngoba ubize uyise noma uyisemkhulu. Ubona ngempela ukuthi uyamazi. omunye uze aliphimise elokuthi uyamazi ngokuthi. 'Wazi mina nsizwa'. 
  Ngiyethemba lezi zinto engithande ukuzichaza lapha ngenhla zizokwenza sazi ukuthi isibongo ngasinye savela kanjani. futhi singadidwa ukuthi yini izibongo zithande 
10 
ukufana kodwa zibe zingahlobene. Koba lula futhi ukuthi sithole ukuthi isibongo esithize sihlobene nasiphi isibongo ngokulandela izithakazelo ezithinta leso sibongo kanye nesinye esihiobene naso. 
  Ngizothanda futhi ukuxolisa ukuthi mina ngokubhala leli bhukwana kangizukuhlaziya ukuthi Ie ndlu ivelaphi nokuthi ivele kanjani. Kodwa okwami ukuthi ngibheke ukuthi isibongo esithize sivelaphi nokuthi sivele kanjani. sihlobene nasiphi isibongo futhi zihlobene kanjani. 
  Ngizozama futhi ukuba ngiveze uliba lwamakhosi alezo zibongo. akudala uma ayekhona. Ngizowaxhuma nawamanje uma esekhona futhi nesikhathi sivuma nanokubambisana nabanikazi baleso naleso sibongo.

Isibongo sakwaZulu sasingaziwa ngap~ambi kweminyaka yawo-1600, ngoba ngaleso sikhathi yayingaziwa indaba yesibongo. Kwakusagqame ukufuduka kakhulu. Lesi sibongo sivela kumaNtungwa Nguni. UMalandela 
UMalandela kuthiwa uzalwa nguLuzumane kaMnguni kaGumede. Bonke laba kasazi ukuthi babekuphi nendawo ngoba uMalandela yena simthola esakhe laphaya ngaphesheya komfula uMhlathuze egqumeni elaziwa ngokuthi kuseMandawe. Wakha umuzi wakhe wawubiza ngokuthi kusoDwini. Wakha lapho ngoba efuna indawo ephakeme. Kodwa akahlalanga lapho isikhathi eside, ngoba wabuye wasuka sengathi amabombo wabuye wawabhekisa emuva, wawela uMhlathuze wenyukela ezintabeni zaseNkwenkwe. 
  Wawela umfula owaziwa ngokuthi kuseMfule uma wediula kancane edolobheni laseMalimede, bediula njalo bakhwela ezintabeni zaseMthonjaneni. behlela emthonjeni woMkhumbane bagudia uPhathe, baze bawela uMkhumbane kanye noNzololo, baze bayofika ngasemfuleni iMpembeni, lapho sibona sengathi uMalandela wabona ukuthi usefikile eKhenani. ngoba kababange besediula lapho. Sengathi yilapho aze akhothamela khona eshiya amadodana akhe agqamile okwakunguQwabe omdala noZulu omncane esandieni sikaNtombela kanye nondiunkulu wakhe uNozinja (UMaGwabini) . 
UZulu 
Ekufeni kukaMalandela kwasala kwaba nombango phakathi kukaQwabe nomnawakhe uZulu. Imbangela yengxabano

  Lezi zinkomo ezibangwayo kwathi ngesikhathi uMalandela esekhona undiunkulu wakhe kwakungumuntu okhuthele kakhulu. Wayethi uma enza imisebenzi yezandia abayifunayo babemnika izimbuzi, yena azishintshanise uma seziziningi ngezinkomo. IsiZulu sithi inkosana kamama indodana encane. 
14 
Ngakho-ke noZulu' wayeyinkosana kanina uNozinja. Ngalokho-ke uNozinja wasikela indodana yakhe encane uphaWu kuzo zonke lezi zinkomo zakhe kanye nezimbuzi. Wayengakwazi lokhu uQwabe. . ngoba engenakuthola lutho efeni likayise.

Ngakho isinqumo samchitha uQwabe, ngalokho wadikila wahamba washiya ikhaya walibhekise ngasolwandle wayokwakha ngaseziNtabeni zoNgoye eduze komfula uMhlathuze. UNdaba 
  UNdaba yindodana kaMageba okwathi esekhotheme yathatha isihlalo sakhe sobukhosi. Esikutholayo ngoNdaba ukuthi nguyena okwaqala ukuzwakala ngokubuthwa 
16 
kwamabutho. Sizwa ngebutho lakhe okwakuthiwa ngaMankankane, kanye nelinye okwakuthiwa ngamaGwadlu. Esikuzwayo futhi ukuthi uNdaba wayengagcini eyinkosi nje kuphela kodwa wayebuye abe yinyanga yezulu. Kuthiwa kwakuthi uma kunesomiso kuhaywe ihubo likaNdaba elalithi: 
UNdaba uyinkosil Ohol 01. Hal Oyel hal Jijijil Ajijil 
  Bathi noma kanjani lalina izulu siphele isomiso. Bathi yinsizwa eyayinobukhulu ubuhlakani. kanti nasebusweni ibukeka. 
  UNdaba wakha unlZI yakhe emmmgi, kodwa mibili eyayibalulekile, kwakungowaseMqekwini (owasendlunkulu) kanye nowaseGazini. wasekhohlwa. Kanti futhi 10 muzi waseGazini yilapho okwakubulawelwa khona izinkomo uma kunemikhosi komkhulu. Laphaya emzini waseGazini inkosana yakhona kwakunguXhoko, bekanye noShwankeni owazala indodakazi uNtopho, yena owazala uMehlana owagcina egane uSenzangakhona kaJama, Kulo muzi waseGazini, kwaphuma abaseMgazini (Ntshangase noBiyela). 
. Siyobuye sixoxe ngalokhu uma sesikhuluma ngabaseMgazini ukuthi bavele kanjani nokuthi baqedwa yini ubuhlobo phakathi kwalezi zibongo. Njengoba sesibona indodakazi kaNtopho uMehlana esegana uSenzangakhona, kodwa bezalana. 
  UNdaba ernzini wakhe waseMqekwini uzale uJama kuSithuli kaNkombane waseMambatheni. UNdaba wakhothama ebuse isizwe sikayise ngobukhulu ubuhlakani. Bathi kayikho inkosi kwangaphambi kwakhe eyayinobuhlakani njengoNdaba indodana kaMageba. kaZulu. ngoba siqala nokuzwa ngaye ngokubuthwa kwamabutho, okusho ukuthi wayesenempi ehlelekile. Wakh'othama uNdaba washiya indodana yakhe uJama. Noma uXhoko ayemdala kodwa ngoba wayesendlini yasekhohlo akakwazanga ukubusa ngoba nguJama owayengowendlu enkulu, ngakho-ke noma emncane ngokuzalwa kodwa ngokwendlu nguyen a owaba nelungelo lokuthatha ubukhosi emva kukayise.

UJama 
  UJama bathi kwakungumuntu omfishane kodwa okhuthele, ozazisayo. Bathi ngumuntu owayenolaka, eshesha ukucasuka. Wayengenandaba namuntu. Bathi wayethanda ukudlala ngomkhonto. Wayekukhonzile ukuciba kangangokuthi esebusa wayedlalela nasekucibeni abantu bakhe. Kwaze kwakhuza amadoda amadala amtshela ukuthi umthetho kawukhethi noma ngabe umuntu uyinkosi engakanani kodwa uyasebenza kuye ungavinjwa yilutho. Wawuyeka-ke 10 mkhuba uJama, wakhula waba yinkosi, kodwa kukhona ukuba yindlovu kayiphikiswa. Wayengatshelwa muntu, sizokuthola lokhu maduze. UJama wayengesiye umuntu ongabungabu ngokuthatha. 
  Uma kushiwo kuthiwa wayenoNdiunkulu oyedwa owamtholela umfana owayebizwa ngokuthi uPhalo. Kodwa akahlalanga isikhathi eside wedlula emhlabeni. 
Okwalandela kwaba ngamantombazana angamawele. 
Ngokwesiko lesiZulu ukutholakala kwamawele kwakusho omkhulu umkhokha ngakho kwakufanele elinye lamawele lendiswe. Manje umuntu okwakufanele akhiphe izwi kwakuyinkosi uqobo. Wabikelwa uJama ngalokhu, kwasengathi uyakuzwa konke abakushoyo. Kuthe uma sekufika izwi lokuthi asho phela ukuthi ngumuphi umntwana ozogingiswa igade, wacela ukuba balethwe kuye azobabona bese esho ukuthi kwendiswa muphi kulaba bantwana. . 
  Esikhundleni sokuthi asho okuIindelekile wawaqamba amagama amawele. Okwakufanele Iigingiswe, waIiqamba ngokuthi nguMkabayi kwathi leIi elinye wathi nguMmama, ngoba laIizothiIe kanti udadewabo wayenameWo ephapheme, athi uma ebuka ngawo uyise washintsha isinqumo sakhe. 
  Kwenzeka insambatheka ngesikhathi isizwe silindele isinqumo senkosi ngengane okufanele igingiswe kodwa uJama "" evele ekhipha izwi lokuthi akukho ngane yakhe ekufanele lokho. Ngamanye amazwi wayesho ukuthi akukho ngane ezobulawa, zizophiia zombili izingane zakhe. Kwala noma izikhulu zezwe kanye naba:fowabo oNkwelo noMWaba," bembonisa ukuthi lokhu kuzodala umkhokha ezweni, lutbo 
18 

kwaba bazishaya ngendlebe etsheni. Wabatshela ukuthi nguyena inkosi futhi abantwana ngabakhe ngakho akukho muntu ozomtshela ukuthi akenzenjani. Uma kukhona umkhokha ongahle uvele uzovelela yena. Okubuhlungu ukuthi umshophi kawuvelelanga yena kodwa wavelela undlunkulu wakhe, ngokuthi wedlula emhlabeni washiya la mawele akhe. 

  Singasho ukuthi kwaba yinduku lena eyashaya udume olukhulu ekhanda IikaJama. Wafa olwembiza ngoba ukhothama nje undlunkulu akashiye mfana ozoba yindlaIifa, noma umuntu oyobusa esikhundleni sakhe uma esekhotheme yena .. ysele" lapha phambi kwakhe namantombazanyana amabIil angasho lutho ngokwesiko lesiZulu. Kwamhlupha lokhu uJama kodwa kwaficakala ukuthi amazwi athi isala kutshelwa sibona ngomopho, kufanele awagwinye eshisa, umntakaNdaba. Neminyaka yayithanda ukuhamba kufanele 

" ~~kosi iganwe. Ukuze phela kutholakale umfana oyothatha . lsikhundla sokubusa izwe uma yona inkosi isikhotheme.

USojiyisa 

  Kuthe uJama isamkhungethe Ie ndaba yokulahlekelwa ngundlunkulu wakhe kanti futhi kukhona nenkinga yokuthi akanayo indlaIifa, waphaka impi eyahamba yayohlasela eB~thonga. Ukuthi kuphi naseButhonga kasazi. Esikwaziyo neSlZoxoxa ngakho isigameko esenzeka. Ekubuyeni kwempi 

, . yakwaZulu, yabuya nezinkomo njengokwejwayelekile kanye nezinto~bi ezinhle. Konke lokhu kwakulethwa ngaphambi kwenkosl yona bese izikhethela ekuthandayo, engakudingi yayikunikeza amabutho ayo. 

,. Kwaba njalo-ke nakuJama, kwalethwa kuyena konke. Phakathi kwezintombi ezazikhona inkosi njengomuntu esishilo 

u~uthi wayengengabungabu ngasesifazaneni wakhangwa ymtombazane eyayiyinhle ingulangaphumasikothe uqobo. 

'ii. Kwakufanele Ie ntombazane ingeniswe esigodlweni sen kosi. Kuthe kusenjalo kwavela enye inhlekelele eyayisandisa .~ashwa kaJama, kuthe ababheki besigodlo senkosi bebona Ie ntombazane kabagcuIiseka ngesimo sempilo yayo. Basola

sengathi izithwele. Nempela yayizithwele. Wabikelwa uJama ngalokhu. Noma kwamphatha kabi kodwa wabuyisa ikhanda lakhe elejwayelekile, waphendula wathi ilunge injalo, izoya esigodlweni. 
  Lokhu abakusolayo okuyihlule uzokujiyisa nakho kube ngumntwana wasendlunkulu. Bakhuza behluleka abomndeni baze bathela bathi ohlaba eyakhe akaphikiswa. Nempela kwatholakala umfana. Noma kwakungemnandl, unembeza umlahla uJama, kodwa ukuthi lona ngumntwana wakhe futhi abekade emlindele. 
  Kwathi ngoba ujiyise ihlule umfana wabizwa ngokuthi nguSojiyisa, uyise kaMaphitha, onguyise kaZibhebhu wakwaMandiakazi onguyise kaBhokwe onguyise kaPhumanyova onguyise kaBhekintinta obusayo njengamanje kwaMandiakazi. 

USenzangakhona 
  Izikhulu zakwaZulu kanye nendlunkulu yonke kwayiphatha kabi ukuzalwa kukaSojiyisa. Kodwa abantu abaphatheka kabi kakhulu kwaba ngamadodakazi kaJama oMkabayi kanye nodadewabo uMmama, ikakhulukazi uMkabayi ngoba nguyena okwakufanele agoduswe kodwa uyise wamvikela esikhundleni sakhe kwakhothama unina amthandayo. Sekuhlangene amadodakazi enkosi kanye nendlunkulu yonke, kwafanele kube khona okwenziwayo ukuvimbela uSojiyisa ukuthi athathe ubukhosi ekukhothameni kwenkosi. 
  Kodwa babelOkuvimbela kanjani lokhu ngoba inkosi yayisishilo yathi ihlule izolijiyisa nalo libe ngumntwana wenkosi njengabo bonke abantwana benkosi. Manje inkosi kayinamfana, isikhulile, isilijiyisile ihlule. . . 
  Phol Kufunekani? Ngumbuzo lona okwakufanele mkosl izibuze wona kanye nezwelana nabo. Kwakufanele kube khona umuntu ozoba nempendulo ezokwenelisa bonke laba bantu, ngoba nesizwe uqobo sasiphatheke kabi, singakaze sikuzwe noma sikubone okunje selokhu kwaba khona ubukhosi bakwaZulu. indodana kaNkwelo umnawenkosi. ukuthi nguye okungeono oyothatha ubukhosi kuSojiyisa.

Noma Ie ntombazana yayindala kunoMkabayi kodwa babengabangani. OMkabayi benodadewabo babemthanda 10 dade, bemthandela ukulunga kwakhe. Le ntombazane igama layo kwakunguMthaniya. UMthaniya wayengomunye wezintombi ezazimisile (engaqomile) elindele ukuthi abazali bakhe bamemulise. Kodwa abantwana benkosi balubeka lonke usizi Iwabo lokushiywa ngunina baeela ukuba azobabheka njengonina wabo. Kasimuzwa uMthaniya ebuza kulaba bantwana ukuthi unina kaSojiyisa uNongiya uzothini. 
  Okwamhlupha kakhulu uMthaniya kwaba' ukuthi inkosi izothini. Lokhu kwakungesiyona inkinga kwiqhalaqhala elinguMkabayi. Lahamba laya kuMudli layombikela ngelikueabangayo benodadewabo. nokuthi sebelungiseni noMthaniya. akwaZulu. Abaningi bakuthatha njengomlingo. Yingakho nje uMthaniya wahlonishwa kangaka kwaZulu, kwaze kwathiwa nezwe elikaMthaniya kuze kube manje, ngoba ebe ngunina walo walizalela inkosi (indlafa). 
UMthaniya wabuye wayizalela inkosi indodakazi uMawa. 
Ekukhothameni kukaJama, uSenzangakhona wayesemncane ukuthi angathatha isihlalo sobukhosi, wayesengumfana wezinkomo. 
  UMkabayi ngokwenqena uSojiyisa wathatha umsebenzi wokubambela umnawakhe isikhundla sobukhosi. Wabeka uMudii ukuba ngumeluleki nondunankulu wakhe. 
  Kwaze kwathi esekhulile uSenzangakhona wathatha i.Ibukhosi kodwa uMkabayi wayebelusile ubukhosi. Okunye okwadala lokho ukuthi uSenzangakhona wayentekenteke, elunge kakhulu, futhi iyinhle Ie nsizwa. Yikho yaganwa kakhulu nje. UMkabayi nodadewabo uMmama kanye noMawa kabazange bagane. Kodwa bagdna sebenernizi ababebusa kuyo, esobuye sixoxe ngayo. 
  USenzangakhona waganwa ngamakhosikazi amaningi akafananga noyise uJama. Waba futhi nernizi eminingi.

AbakwaQwabe 

Abantu bakwaQwabe uma ukhuluma ngomlando wabo kufana nokuthi uphindaphinda umlando wakwaZulu ngoba imvelaphi yabo iyefana. Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi uQwabe uzalwa nguMalandela kanye noZulu. Ngakho abantu bakwaQwabe badabuka kuMalandela njengabakwaZulu. 
  Kuzokhumbuleka futhi ukuthi ekuxabaneni kwala madodana kaMalandela, uQwabe okuyindodana enkulu wahamba walibhekisa ngasolwandle waze wakha eduze 
35 







36 

I 




~-I 
z ...• 
o 
g 


komfula uMhlathuze ngaphansi kwezintaba zoNgoye. Wakha umuzi wakhe wathi kuseMthandeni ebhinqa abakubo ngoba ethi kabamthandanga waze wehlukana nabo, ngakho-ke wayesethi kwafikela kubo kabamthande. 
  Kuthiwa isizwe sikaQwabe sanda kakhulu kangangokuba saphindwa kathathu uma siqhathaniswa nesomnawakhe. Kuthiwa sasisuka emngceleni wesizwe sakwaMthethwa siyofika esizweni sakwaDube ngasolwandle, siphinde siyofika ehiathini laseNkandia. Bese lehla liyokhawula ngomfula uMhlathuze. Nizokhumbula futhi ukuthi uMalandela wasuka eMandawe waya eBabanango, nakhu nendodana yakhe uQwabe sesimthola eduze kwalezi zintaba zaseMandawe. Abantu bakwaQwabe babebizwa ngokuthi abakwaNozidiya ngoba amakhosikazi akhona ayefaka izidiya. 
	Ngesikhathi 	sekubusa 	uDingiswayo 	kwaMthethwa, 
kwaQwabe kwase kubusa uKhondio. Ebusela kuwo umuzi kakhokho wakhe eMthandeni. NoPhakathwayo indodana kaKhondio yasebenzisa umuzi kayise uMthandeni. Kuthe uma uShaka ehiasela uPhakathwayo, abantu bakwaQwabe bathutha bayokwakha ngaphesheya koThukela eduze nomfula uMvoti. Ngokukhumbula umuzi omkhulu okwakuyisigodlo esihlonishwa nguye wonke umuntu wakwaQwabe omncane nomdala, omusha nosekhulile, owesilisa nowesifazane, ngoba kwakungumuzi wawokhokho babo, kwathi ekusukeni kwabo bewela uThukela bafike bakha omunye uMthandeni phakathi kwakwaMaphumulo nakwaDukuza. 
  Noma singeke sibalandelisane bonke, kuze kufike kule nkosi ekhona njengamanje kodwa ukusuka phezulu ubukhosi bakwaQwabe busuka kuQwabe uqobo. 
	AbakwaKhuzwayo 	.'i 
AbakwaKhuzwayo bavela kuKhuzwayo indodana kusengathi kaMahlobo kaSimamane. Kwakufanele ukuba kube nguyena uKhuzwayo othatha ubukhosi bakwaQwabe kodwa ngasizathu simbe akwenzekanga lokho ngoba bathi uKhuzwayo kwasebuncaneni wayezazisa, futhi ekubeka ngokukhulu

50. 
ukuqhosha lokhu ukuthi uyoba yinkosi ekukhothameni kukayise. Wayenza nje izinto ezingathandeki ekhuzwa njalo, kodwa kube nhlanga zemuka nomoya nje. Yikho aze athola leli gama lokuthi nguKhuzwayo, ngoba ekhuzwa njalo. Lokhu kwamfakela esikhulu isigcwagcwa ernndenini. Kuthe sekufanele kukhonjwe' ozothatha ubukhosi ekukhothameni kukayise, kwakhonjwa umnawakhe uLufutha. Kwamthukuthelisa lokhu uKhuzwayo wasuka kwelakubo wawela umfula iNonoti eyozifunela amadJelo aluhlaza ezweni elalivulekile lingenamuntu. 
  Wakha ngaphesheya kweNonoti kwehle njalo kuze kuyofika eNingizimu yoThukela. Abantu bonke ahamba nabo ababange besabizwa ngokuthi ngabakwaQwabe kodwa kwase kuthiwa ngabakwaKhuzwayo. Lokhu kwase kuyimpinda kubantu bakwaQwabe ukuba enye yamadodana akhona adube ikhaya ayozakhela esawo isibongo. Sizomkhumbula noQwabe ukuthi wehlukana kanjani nekubo wadela ubuzibulo. Nokuthi sona lesi sibongo sakwaQwabe sadaleka kanjani. Sekuphinde uMansumpa-ke. 
  Lokhu kusafakazela khona esaqala ngakho ukuthi izibongo zonke zidabuka emagameni abantu. Ngisho noma ngabe igama lomuntu lavela kanjani, isizukulwane sakhe kasinandaba nalokho kodwa sifuna ukumdumisa umsunguli wesibongo sabo. Nabantu bakwaKhuzwayo kababanga nandaba nokuthi leli gama likayisemkhulu laqambeka kanjani.' Namuhla sinabantu bakwaKhuzwayo abaziqhenyayo ngesibongo sabo. Bayasithanda futhi kakhulu. 
Ake sibelamanise abantu bakwaKhuzwayo.

AbakwaSibiya 
Abantu bakwaSibiya bangabanye abangamaNtungwa Nguni; ngoba nabo bangabendJu kaMalandela njengoZulu noQwabe. Kodwa sengathi bathanda ukwencika kakhulu kuQ,:,,~iJe kunoZulu. Ngikusho lokhu ngoba abantu bakwaSIbIya bazihlanganisa noQwabe ngesithakazelo esithi Gumede Mnguni. kanti abakaZulu bona kabasisebenzisi lesi sit~ak?zelo .. 
  Ukudabuka kwabantu bakwaSibiya kusukela ezmSIzwem eziyizelamani uZembethe kanye noZingelwayo. Bobabili sengathi babengabafowabo bakaQwabe noZulu kodwa kwenye indJu. UZingelwayo kwakungomdala kanti uZembethe kungornncane. UZembethe wahamba wayokwakha eduze nomfula uMkhumbane kanti uZingelwayo wakha eMthonjaneni egqumaneni elaziwa ngokuthi kuseGumeni. Wakha khona ebone ihlanze elehla njalo lize liyofika ezimfundeni zomfula iMfolozi emhlophe. Kuleli hlanze kwakugcwele izinyamazane iphekwa ngomhluzi wenye. Babona ukuthi nezinkomo zizobachuma lapha abantu bakaZingelwayo. Babona ukuthi sebefike kwelingafelwa nkonyane. Nangempela zabachuma izinkomo nayo yonke imfuyo abayifuya kuleya ndawo. .. . 
  lzinkomo kwakunguchibidolo uqobo, zIbulala myoka. BathI zanda ngale ndJela yokuthi zase zingalingani esibayeni, ezakhelwe sona. Zazithi uma zibuyiswe emaqeleni. zigcwale isibaya ezinye zikake umuzi. 
  Abantu ababedlula ngendJela babezibuka lezi zinkomo bezwe amakhosikazi ethokoza ethi: "Nampo-ke abakwaSibiya ngenkomo abanye bebiya ngamahlahla", besho ngoba izinkomo zikake umuzi. Yilapho-ke okwazaleka khona isibongo 
sakwaSibiya. Yonke inzalo 	kaZingelwayo 	kwathiwa 
ngeyakwaSibiya, kodwa 	kabayekanga 	ukuthi'

isibongo ngegama. Kuthiwa futhi laba bantu babuye bahlangana. baba yisizwe esisodwa sakwaSibiya. Futhi kwase kukhona nokuganiselana ngoba sizokhumbula uMthaniya indodakazi kaManyelela Sibiya isigana uJama kuze kuzalwe uSenzangakhona. uyise woShaka noDingane kanye noMpande, ababusa izwe lakwaZulu. Ngenxa yezimpi zikaShaka abantu bakwaSibiya nabo bahlakazeka bagcwala lonke leli likaMthaniya. Sesibathola laphaya nalaphaya. 
  Okwenza ukuthi laba bantu bakwaSibiya banganyamalali njengezinye izizwe ukuthi basheshe bayibona ingozi yokuma phambi kukaShaka ukuthi kwakungukuzishabalalisa isibili. Ngakho bathatha amabutho abo bawethula kuShaka. wandisa ngawo impana yakhe eyayisencane ngaleso sikhathi. 
Ake sibheke ukwelamana kwamakhosi akwaSibiya.

AbakwaMakhanya 
Abantu bakwaMakhanya bahlobene kakhulu nabantu bakwaKhuzwayo. Ngingasho nje ukuthi abakwaMakhanya nabakwaKhuzwayo bayinto eyodwa, ngoba isigameko esiveze isibongo sakwaMakhanya sisukela emndenini wakwaKhuzwayo. Nabo bazazi bengoMnguni kaGumede. 
	Kuthiwa 	ngesikhathi 	kwehlukana 	abakwaQwabe 
nabakwaKhuzwayo, basuka abakwaKhuzwayo bayokwakha phakathi koThukela neNonoti. Kodwa kwakuthi njalo uma kunemikhosi efuna isizwe bawele bonke uThukela baye ezweni lakwaQwabe lapho kwakunekomkhulu khona. 
  Ngakho kwase kunomndeni wakwaKhuzwayo owase uwele iNonoti. Kwakuthi njalo uma kukhona umkhosi komkhulu Ie mindeni yakwaKhuzwayo ilindane ukuze ikhukhule kanyekanye isiya komkhulu. Kwathi ngomunye unyaka kuzo?a nomkhosi. Ie mindeni yamemana njengokujwayelekile. Kant! kababuzanga elangeni. ngalolo suku ebusuku lana kakhulu imvula. kwagcwala imifula. Uma sekufanele kuhanjwe kuyiwe komkhulu. kwatholakala ukuthi laba abangaphesheya komfula kabakwazi ukuwela. Babalinda babalinda laba abanye lutho ukufika. 
  Uma bezobabheka bathola ukuthi umfula mila izindwani kawuweleki. Babona abafowabo bemi ngaphesheya bakhe umkhanya, bejiyelwe ukuthi benzenjani. Base bethi laba abanye. hhayi-ke ngeke sisanilinda. salani ninjalo, nakhe umkhanya lowo. Kusukela lapho laba bantu baziwa ngokuthi ngabakwaMakhanya. ngoba balibala ukwakha umkhanya engabe bazama isu lokuwela umfula ukuze kuyiwe komkhulu. 
Kuthiwa abakwaMakhanya babuye behlukana kabili. 
Kukhona okwathi abanye bebaleka beqa uThukela. ngesikhathi sikaDingane. kwakhona abasalayo. Bona bakha laphaya eduze kwaseMpaphala ngaseNtumeni eShowe abazibiza ngokuthi ngabaseMambedwini. bakaMdingi. kanti ababalekela ulaka lukaDingane ngabakaNqetho. UNqetho wabaleka nabalandeli bakhe waze wayofika kwelikaFaku eMampondweni.

AbakwaKhwela 
Abantu bakwaKhwela bangabanye bendlu kaQwabe. Noma bengabalulekile emiandweni kangangokuthi abanye baze bathi akusiwona amaZulu kahle ngoba bengazelwa lutho. AbaMbo (Dlamini) 
Kade sikhuluma ngabaNtungwa sonke lesi sikhathi, ake sicaphune futhi nakubeNguni baseMbo, ngoba izibongo eziningi zalapha zixhumeke kulesi sigaba. Uma sikhuluma 
42 


ngabeNguni baseMbo sikhuluma ngesizukulwane sikaMumbo indoda okuthiwa yasuka enhla nezwe yalibangisa ngasendaweni esibizwa manje ngokuthi kuseMozambiki, kwelaMashangane. Kodwa kabazinzanga lapho babuye bafuduka baze bayofika eduze nezintaba zoBombo, bathiya ngomfula uPhongolo lapho kwaba khona enkulu inhlukano. Abanye bacabanga ukuwela uPhongolo kodwa abanye bakhetha ukusala, noma baphindele emuva. Abanye bona bafisa ukudundubala izintaba zoBombo, bayosithela ngale kwazo b.efuna amadlelo aluhlaza, nokufuna inkululeko, ngoba base bande kakhulu. Nalabo nalabo sebefuna ukuzimela, bazakhele isizwana sabo abazosibusa kalula. Kulaba bantu bakaMumbo kukhona abantu ababa ngamaZulu kanti kukhona ababa ngamaSwazi abanye baba ngamaThonga. Kodwa bonke laba bantu basuka emnyombweni owodwa kaMumbo. 
	Abantu 	abasala 	nokuthi 	ngabasEmbo, 	ngabantu 
bakwaMkhize. Balingisa abantu bakwaQwabe, okwaba yibona bodwa abasebenzisa uMnguni Gumede, ngokugqamiIe. Uma ubheka esihlokweni esingenhla. ngithe abaMbo, ngase ngitbi kubakaki, Dlamini. Lokhu ngikushiso ukuthi abantu abangabeNguni baseMbo bonke baxhume kuDlamini. Lapha sithola kuqhamuka izibongo eziningi, ezilapha kwaZulu neziseSwazini kanye naseButhonga. Lokhu sizokuveza ngesikhathi sichaza ukuzalana kwalezi zizwe. 
AMalangeni 
AMalangeni sengathi iyona nzalabantu, kulesi sigaba ngoba uma sicwaninga sehla nabo sithola kuphuma izizwe eziningi ezingumgogodla walapha kwaZulu. Cabanga nje ngesibongo esikhulu sakwaZulu, uNdwandwe. Ucabange ngesibongo sakwaMkhize. Ungacabanga nangesibongo sakwaHadebe, AmaHlubi, kanye nabo bonke .oDlamini abalapha kweIikaMthaniya. Ucabange futhi ngoGumede kaManukuza waseButhonga. Zonke lezi zibongo zingumnyombo waMalangeni. Abanye bazodideka bathi yingani ngikhulume ngabantu baseSwazini. Isizathu yilesi esengisibekile ngenhla sokuthi izibongo esinazo lapha zixhumeke lapha.

Kanti futhi kuningi ebesingakuxoxa ukuba besinaso isikhathi sokwenza lokho. kodwa ngenxa yokuthi isikhathi kasikho kahle, sizokwedlulela ezibongweni ezithinta leli likaMthaniya. 
AbakwaNdwandwe 
Abantu bakwaNdwandwe baqala ukugqama ngesikhathi sekubusa uZwide indodana kaLanga. Ngale kukaZwide akukho okubalulekile esikutholayo ngaphandle kwemvelaphi yabo. Kuthiwa abantu bakwaNdwand"'(e njengoba sekuvelile ukuthi baWobene nabakwaNgwane. uLanga indodana kaXaba kaLudonga yahamba nomfowabo balibhekisa ngasoPhongolo. 10 mfowabo kwakunguNgwane II indo dana kaDlamini II. kuthe uma sebefika oPhongolo. uNgwane wabuyela emuva ngasezintabeni zaseMbilane, lapho afike wafela khona. 
  Wangcwatshwa lapho nezizukulwane zakhe. Kuze kube manje leya ntaba yathathwa njengentaba engewele. Kuze kube manje abantu baseSwazini bangewaba amakhosi nezikhulu zabo kule ntaba eWala njalo iqashiwe. 
  ULanga-ke yena wawela uPhongolo waze wayofika entabeni yaseMagudu. Yilapho afike wafela khona. eshiya indodana yakhe uZwide. Ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaZwide kwakubusa uNdungunya eSwazini. owayenguyise kaSobhuza wokuqala amzala kuSomjelusa. uLasimelane. Abantu bakwaNdwandwe banda baba yisizwe esikhulu ngaphansi kukaZwide. Ngenxa yokwanda kwesizwe sakwaNdwandwe. uZwide waphoqeka ukuba abuthe abafana abasebancane ukuba babe ngamabutho ukuze bakwazi ukuvikela izwe lakwaNdwandwe. elase lande kakhulu ngoba umngcele walo wawusuka phezu koPhongolo, kuyoma ngeMfolozi emnyama, kwehle njalo kuze kuyofika eSikhwebezi. eduze kwehlathi laseNgome. kuphinde kwehle kuyoshaya ngasolwandle kwiSt. Lucia Bay. UZwide elinye igama likayise ngaphandle kukaLanga kwakunguMkhatshwa wokuqala. 
45 




53. 
  Ngike ngasho ukuthi isizwe sakwaNdwandwe sasikhula sindlondlobala ngaphansi kukaZwide, kwaba yisizwe esasesabeka kakhulu kwaZulu, izizWe zisazimele lingakazihlanganisi iLembe. Kwakuyisona isizwe esikhulu kanye nesakwaMthethwa ngaphansi kukaDingiswayo kalobe. bese kuba ngesakwaQwabe ngaphansi kukaPhakathwayo. Abantu bakwaNdwandwe babesatshwa njengabantu abanemilingo, nabazi kakhulu ngezintelezi. 
  Kodwa umlando usitshela ukuthi uZwide inkosi yabakwaNdwandwe yayingazi lutho ngemithi nemilingo ababeyisho,. kodwa ngunina uNtombazi owayazi kakhulu, ngamakhambi. Ngakho wonke umbuso kaZwide namandla akhe onke ayencike kunina. Bathi kwakukhona nodadewabo owayeyinyanga yezulu, uMadungudu. Bathi wayelibele yilesi siphiwo sakhe ebizwa izwe lonke ukuba azonisa izulu, kangangokuthi waze waphuthelwa yinto ebalulekile empilweni yakhe umendo, (Phela wayesesabeka kangangokuthi izinsizwa zonke zase zimesaba.) Unina kaZwide uNtombazi wayedume ngokuthi uma indodana yakhe ikade ilwa nenkosi ethize, inqanyulwe ikhanda. liyobekwa lihlobise indlu yakhe, lokho ethi kuzonika uZwide amandla okunqoba izitha zakhe, kalula. Nempela uZwide wanqoba amakhosi amaIiingi abangaphansi kwakhe. 
  Ukuze alibuse kahle izwe lakhe uZwide wakha ihlalankosi lakhe walibiza ngokuthi kukwaNongoma, 10 Nongoma osekhona namanje osulidolobha. Le ndawo yayiphakathi nendawo ezindaweni ayesezinqobile. sizibalile ngenhla lezi zindawo. Unina wamakhela owakhe umuzi wakwaDiovunga. Lo muzi wawukade ukoMbuzi, kodwa ngenxa yokuthi kusehlanzeni kakhulu wawuthutha wawakha ngaphansi kwentaba iThokazi. Yilapho-ke amakhanda amakhosi ayephelela khona. 
  Ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaZwide kwakukhona indlu encane yakwaNdwandwe, indlu kaManukuza, umfowabo kaMavuso kaLanga wokuqala owayebuye abizwe ngokuthi nguMkhatshwa wokuqala. Indlu kaManukuza yaziwa ngokuthi ngeyakwaNxumalo kuze kube manje. 
46 


  Lesi sibongo bathi savela ngokuba uManukuza eshonelwe ngunina esemncane. kwase kuthi abazanyane bakhe bamncelisa umnxumo. Bathi yayiminingi iminxumo, kangangokuthi kwathi uManukuza esekhulile esaqhubeka nokuncela umnxumo. wadideka ukuthi uzoncela muphi, base bemdlalisa bephethe Ie minxumo becula bethi, 'Nxuma 10 nxuma 10'. Kwase kuthiwa nguNxumalo uzalo lonke Iwakhe kwabe sekuthiwa olwakwaNxumalo. 
Saqina lesi sibongo kwase kuthiwa yindlu yasekhohlo. 
Okunye okuzwakalayo kuthiwa kwathi kunomcimbi endlini enkulu njengokujwayelekile zonke izindlu kwakufanele zilethe nazo amaqhaga kanye nezipheko. Kwasuka izintombi zendlu kaManukuza zahambisa utshwala endlini enkulu yakwaNdwandwe. 
  Kuthiwa owayebusa ngaleso sikhathi kwaNdwandwe kwakunguMavuso, owakhangwa ngenye yamantombazane asendlini yakubo encane, wayithanda wayithatha yamgana kwala noma sebekhuza abomndeni bethi akwenziwa lokhu kodwa kwaba nhlanga zemuka nomoya kuMavuso wansondo egajwe uthando. Wathi uma eziphendulela Ie ndlu sekungeyakwaNxumalo. llapho-ke la saqina khona isibongo sakwaNxumalo. UZwide ubusa nje uyakwazi lokhu. indaba isizophinde yonakale fl,lthi uma uMalusi indodana kaMkhatshwa wesibili isithatha udadewabo kaDingiswayo inkosi yakwaMthethwa, okwakuyinkukhu nempaka phakathi kwayo noZwide. UZwide wagxeka uMalusi ngokuthi ungumfowabo kodwa usemdayise kuDingiswayo ngokuganwa ngudadewabo abayizitha naye. 
Kwadaleka obukhulu ubutha phakathi kwakhe noMalusi. 
Okunye futhi okwenza ukuba kwande igebe phakathi kukaZwide nomfowabo uMalusi kwaba ngukuthi, uZwide benonina uNtombazi bafune ukuhunga uDingiswayo ukuze bamthonye atholakale kalula, kwafuneka ukuba kube khona umuntu ozoyocwiya insila kaDingiswayo. Kwathi itulo elakhiwa kwaba ngelokuhambisa izintombi ziyogana uDingiswayo. UZwide wakhipha udadewabo uNtombazana ukuba ayomakhela ubuhlobo nenkosi yakwaMthethwa. Kepha

eTalagubhe. Kuthe emva kwalokho basuka bagudla ulwandle ngaseMpumalanga, behla njalo bebheke ngaseNingizimu, baze bafika eChwebeni (St. Lucia Bay). Njengabantu abafuye kakhulu babethanda ukuthi imfuyo yabo iklabe lapho kunamazolo khona. 
Kodwa amazolo ayezotholakala kanjani eduze nolwandle? 
Kwaba kubantu baseMbo ukuthi bafunc indawo engcono. Ngakho bahamba ezindaweni eziphakeme ezihlala njalo zinemikhizo. Kuthiwa bahamba njalo baze bayofika ezintabeni zaseQhudeni. Ngenxa yokuthi laba bantu babehamba ezindaweni ezinemikhizo, kwase kuthiwa ngabakwaMkhize. 
  Bafika laphaya eQhudeni sebeke bazinza emahlathini aseNgome. Laphaya eQhudeni bakha kusuka ehlathini laseQhudeni kuze kuyofika emfuleni iNsuze, kanti ngaseNtshonalanga bavinjwa uThukela, kwathi ngaseNyakatho bavinjwa nguMzinyathi. Kwathi ukuba uZihlandlo abone omakhelwane bakhe abanamandla kakhulu kunaye bebhuqwabhuqwa nguShaka, baze banyamalala phambi kwakhe, futhi kuyizizwe ezinamandla wavele wenza ubuhlakani bokuphephisa isizwe sakwaMkhize olakeni lukaShaka ngokuba ayozikhonzela kuye, wazakhela obukhulu ubuhlobo, okwaze kwagoduka iLembe bengabangani. Kuthiwa uZihlandlo wayesevakashela njalo kwaDukuza, ukuyokotha inkosi yakhe uShaka, esuka ernzini wakhe kwaNyakenye ngaphesheya koThukela. Kuthiwa nguyen a rnuntu wokuqala owabona umuntu ornhlophe. Bathi wayethi yena yishaywa (laba bantu abamhlophe). Kanti ngurnlungu (u-Isaacs).   Bonke oDlamini imvamisa yabo ivela kuDlamini wolibo IwakwaNgwane (AMASWAZI). ODlamini esinabo imvamisa yabo bangaManguni aseMbo (Embo Nguni). Ngakho-ke labo Dlamini baseNatali bahlobene noMkhize, amaHlubi, nabakwaNgwane, bangabahlobo futhi baxhumene. NgoDlamini bakaNyanya, bona abathe ukwehluka kulaba abanye ngemvelaphi yabo. Umsuka woDlamini laba engizokhuluma ngabo sengishilo ngathi bavela kwaNgwane, ngempela bavela khona kwaNgwane. Nizokhumbula ukuthi ngesikhathi sikhuluma ngolibo lwamakhosi akwaNgwane, sakhuluma ngoDlamini wokuqala indodana kaCebisa. Kukuyena 10 Dlamini lapho kuxhuma khona ulibo 10Dlamini. Sichaza lapha izindlu ngokwehlukana kwazo. 
	UDlamini 	waseSwazini, 	yilo 	Dlamini 	okuthiwa 
nguMlangeni. Bonke oDlamini basebukhosini baseSwazini kuthiwa ngaMalangeni. Ngisho nemali yakhona kuthiwa Lilangeni noma Amalangeni uma isiningi. Babuye babizwe ngokuthi abakwaNkosi, kulandelwa uNkosi wokuqala indodana kaSidwabaseluthuli. Kodwa kababasebenzisi oLusibalukhulu, oMalandela kanye nabanye. Ngakho-ke sizobashiya labo Dlamini baseSwazini, siqhubeke nalaba baseNatali nakwaZulu, sibone ukuthi bahlobene kanjani. 
  Kuthiwa uDlamini wokuqala wazala amadodana amahlanu abalulekile. Ngithi abalulekile ngoba yilapho kuvela khona izindlu zakwaDlamnini. Indlu enkulu yiyona lena eseSwazini. Yona ivela endodaneni endala kaDlamini wokuqala uMnyambane. Nguyena ozala oDlamini beKunene. Kube khona abaseMakhuzeni, kube khona abakwaBhidla, kube khona abaSesiphahleni, bese kuba khona abaseNhlangwini.

AMAHLUBI 
Abantu baseMahlutshini bangabaseMbo. Ngamanye amagama bangaBambo Nguni. Lokho kusho ukuthi bahlobene noDlamini laba esike sakhuluma ngabo. sathi ngabaseSwazini 
- kanye nabaseNatali. Noma betholakala behlezi phakathi nezwe. kodwa ulimi Iwabo Iwalubadalula ukuthi akusiwo kahle aMantungwa Nguni. Nemvunulo yabo yayibachaza. ukuthi baphuma eSwazini. 
  Laba bantu kuze kuthiwe ngaMahlubi kususelwa kwenye yamakhosi akwaNgwane eyayinegama elinguHlubi. indodana kaLudonga wokuqala. Lokhu okugcizelela khona ukuthi ubuhlobo bukhulu. Vma bemchaza 10 muntu ababengamazi. bathi wayenombala omhlophe okwesithwathwa. enezinwele ezinde sengathi yishoba lenkomo. Noma nabo babedumile ngezinwele ezinde kodwa ezabo kwakuthiwa yimiyeko. yikho kwaze kwathiwa yiziYendane. Bathi 10 muntu wayenezinyawo ezivalekile kuthi uma enyathela esihlabathini unyawo lubishe. uBhungane. Yingakho nje simthola eboleka 10Iu godo kulo mlisa ukuba ayolusebenzisa ekubulaleni inkosi yaMangwane. Bathi wathi esentabeni lapho okwakufanele asebenzise khona loIu godo esithola kamuva ukuthi kwakuyisibhamu somlungu, wafike waqala ukudubula. AbakwaTembe 
	Abantu 	bakwaTembe 	badabuka 	phakathi 	nezwe 
laseMozambikwe. Noma-ke umlando usitshela ukuthi imvelaphi yabo impela isenkabeni yezwe lapho kwadabuka khona izizwe eziningi. Kodwa esikutholayo ngesizwe sakwaTembe ukuthi sidabuka kuleli zwekazi. Kuthiwa babakhe phakathi kwemifula iMabhudu kanye noMtembe. Sengathi yilo mfula owaveza igama abantu bakwaTembe ababizwa ngalo, ngoba kuthiwa ekufikeni kwabo ngasogwini lolwandle babe sebebizwa ngabakwaTembe. 
Isizwe sakwaTembe sasehlukene kabili ngobundlu baso. 
Kwakukhona indlu enkulu eyayakhe phakathi komfula iMabhudu kanye nolwandle. Kwathi ekugcineni kwathiwa ngokwesiko lena yindlu encane. Kasazi ukuthi lokhu kwashiwolani. Kuthiwa laba bantu babekhuthele belima, befuye nezinkomo. Kanti laba, okwagcina sekuthiwa iyona ndlu enkulu, babakhe phakathi kwemifula iMabhudu kanye noMtembe. Kuthiwa inhlalo yalaba yayingahlelekile. Bengakhuthele nakakhulu. Impilo yabo yayencike kakhulu kule ndlu abathi ingencane, ngokudla nangohwebo. 
  Kuthiwa abantu bakwaTembe babetshala ummbila, ubhatata. amantongomane, izindumba (Imbumba). Babedumile futhi nangemisebenzi 'I yezandla. Babencibilikisa insimbi nethusi, ababekumba phansi. Lokhu babenza ngakho amageja okulima, bakha izimbazo, imikhonto, amasongo nezinye izinto zokuhloba. 
  Kanti babaziwa futhi nasekubazeni amabhodwe, izingqoko, izinkezo, izixembe kanye nezinye izitsha ezakhiwa ngokhuni.

Nendawo 	abakhe 	kuyona 	kuthiwa 	iMabhuduland 
(Maputaland) . 
  Kuthe ngesikhathi sokukhothama kukaHluma, kwathi omunye wabafowabo uNonkantsha wafuna ukubeka enye yamadodana omfowabo uMakhasanyana esikhundleni sikaHluma, esikhundleni sokuba kubekwe indlalifa kaHluma enguNoziyingili. Yilokhu-ke okwenza ukuba uNoziyingili abaleke kwelakubo wayocela usizo enkosini yakwaZulu okwakunguMpande ngaleso sikhathi. UMpande wawathumela amabutho akhe ayeholwa nguNongqiwu indodana kaMgobhozi wakwaMsane. 
Yabambana phezu kukaNondaka umfula ongenela oSuthu. 
Wabulawa-ke uNonkantsha nalona ayembeka uMakhasanyana. Wasithatha-ke isikhundla sakhe uNoziyingili. Kwathi ekukhothameni kukaNoziyingili, kwathatha esikhundleni sakhe indodana yakhe uNgwanase. Kuthiwa sengathi nguyena owaba ngumqambi wangempela weTongaland Kingdom (Umbuso wamaThonga) ngonyaka ka 1887. 
  Lo mbuso wawusakhelwe khona eMozambikwe, kodwa kwase kuqalile ukubusa kwaMaputukezi ngaleso sikhathi. Kwaba khona ukushayisana phakathi kwamaPutukezi namakhosi ayebusa kule ndawo eseqala ukwandisa umbuso wawo. Kwathi ngo-1890, aqala ukuxosha amakhosi endawo angavurni ukuthela kuwo. 
  UZambili indodakazi kaSobhuza inkosi yaseSwazini ongunina kaNgwanase wathatha uNgwanase (owayesemncane ngaleso sikhathi esizwa nguyena unina ekubuseni) wabaleka naye waya ngakwaZulu, waze wafika kwaNongoma enkantolo yakhona sekuphethe izimantshi zamaNgisi. 
  Imantshi eyayikhona ngaleso sikhathi uMnu. Foxon, wamthatha uNgwanase nabantu bakhe wayobabeka endaweni ephakathi nePhelindaba kanye nechwebakazi iKhosi (Kosi bay) lapho bafike bahlala khona ngokuthula, kuze kube manje. Sebaziwa njengabantu bakwaMhlabuyalingana, eMaputa kwaNgwanase.

58. 
uMkhulutshani. Kuthe ekufeni kukaDingane, uZikhali wathola intuba yokunyomuka kwaZulu. Wawela umfula uMkhuze wahamba njalo waze wayozinza eSwazini. Wafike waganwa indodakazi yeNkosi uSobhuza uNomialazi, okwathi uma eSwazini sekwakhiwa uzungu lokubulala uZikhali, uNomlalazi washeshe wakwazi lokhu wase emvusa umyeni wakhe. 
  Wabaleka-ke uZikhali, wathi ubuyela kwaZulu wafica sekudlange amaBhunu, noma uMpande wayebusa kodwa amabhunu ayesefake ikhala embusweni wakwaZulu. Yingakho nje asuka wayozifunela amadlelo aluhlaza kule ndawo yakwaMbila. 
  Ngesikhathi uZikhali eshona eNyakatho nolwandle abanye bona baqonda ezintabeni Zokhahlamba. Lapho amaNgwane azibiza ngokuthi ngawakwaHiongwane. Isizwe sakwaMbila noma sithi, isizwe sakwaZikhali sakhelene nezizwe eziningi kodwa esibalulekile. ngesizibiza ngokuthi ngesakwaMabaso Nxumalo. 
    INYANOA 
Abantu bakwaZikhali 
Abantu bakwaZikhali bangaMaNgwane, ahlobene naMaNgwane kaMatiwane. Empeleni abantu bakwaZikhali baqhamuka eSwazini kwaNgwane. AmaNgwane esiwathola manje oKhahlamba ayazalana nala MaNgwane akwaZikhali. Eduze kwechibi lakwaSibhayi (Lake Sibayi) kunendawo lapho ebizwa ngokuthi kukwaMbila. Kasazi kahle ukuthi leli gama lavelaphi, ngoba laphaya kunezinto ezimbili ezibizwa ngaleli gama. Sizokhumbula ummbila odliwayo, notshalwayo, kugaywe impuphu. Kanti kukhona umuthi ozimilela endle abantu bakuleya ndawo abawubiza ngokuthi ummbila. Kunenyamazane futhi ehlala ezixhotsheni eyaziwa ngokuthi imbila. Manje kasiqondi-ke ukuthi igama okubizwa ngalo Ie ndawo livela kuphi kulokhu esengikubalile. Lokhu ngikusho ngoba kuleya ndawo miningi imithi ebizwa ngaleli gama ikakhulukazi uma usubheke ngasolwandle. 
  Ngokunjalo futhi nommbila yisitshalo sokU(jala esatshalwa lapha kule ndawo. Ngakho-ke kukhomba ukuthi zombili lezi zigigaba kungaba yizona ezidale ukuba Ie ndawo ibizwe ngokuthi kukwaMbila. Kulesi sifmida sakwaMbila kuhlala isizwe sakwaZikhali. Ngokomlando kuthiwa lesi sizwe sadabuka eSwazinL Kuthiwa sasakhe eduze nomfula uPhongolo ngesikhathi kubusa iNkosi uDingane kwaZulu. Umuntu owayengumholi wabo kwakunguZikhali. 
  Ngenxa yokuthi babaziwa ngokuthi bangabantu bakaZikhali kwagcina sekuthiwa ngabakwaZikhali. Abantu bakwaZikhali 
	noma bethathwa 	ngokuthi ngaMathonga 
	akwaMhlabuyalingana 	kodwa ukudabuka kwabo 
kubahlobanisa namaNguni aseMbo (Embo Nguni). Ngoba bahlobene nabaseSwazini kanye namaNgwane kaMatiwane. Phela uZikhali indodana kaMatiwane. Ngokubaleka kukaMatiwane, ebalekela uDingane kanti uyogcina embulele, abantu bakaZikhali behla njalo bona baqonda ngasolwandle. Kodwa ekubulaweni kukaMatiwane uDingane wayiphephisa impilo kazikhali owayesengurnfanyana omncane kangangokuthi waze wabuthwa wangeniswa ebuthweni

AbaseLangeni 
Abantu baseLangerti bangabanye abantu ababaluleke kakhulu emlandweni wesizwe sakwaZulu. Sengathi ukudabuka kwabo kuhlobene kakhulu nabantu bakwaNdwandwe, yize noma 
	babakhelene nabantu bakwaZulu. 		. 
	Lokhu 	kusibuyisela 	ekuthini 	abantu 	baseLangeru 
bangaMaNguni aseMbo. Lokhu kuthatha u~~t~i sikholelwe kukhona ngenxa yokuthi, abantu baseSwazllll mdlu enkulu yakhona kuthiwa ngeyaseLangeni.. Kukhulunywa laphay~ ngamaLangeni (Dlamini Mlangem). Abantu baseLangem kasibazi ukuthi bafuduka kanjani besuka Ie kwelakwaNgwane, ngoba thina sesibathola laphaya eMithine~de, . bakhe endaweni esuka khona eMithinemide lze lyov~la ngoMhlathuze, yehle ngezintaba zoNdundulu kuze kuyofika 
eNkwalini. . 
Abantu baseLangeni njengamanje sebezibiza ngokuthl 
bangabakwaMhlongo ngenxa yegama lomunye uyise~ul~ wabo owayebizwa ngokuthi nguMhiongo. r:'gesl~athl seLembe abantu baseLangeni babezibusa bebuswa YJnkOSI yabo uMakhedama owaba yiNjomane eyaduka inJinyak~nyaka. Kanti abantu baseLangeni babaluleke kakhulu ngoba iLembe lona uqobo lalizalwa khona eLangeni, lizal~a yinkosazana kaBhebhe, okunguyena owaziwa ngokuthl nguMhlongo. Owayakhe umuzi wakhe waseBozeni. eganwe nguMfunda wakwaQwabe, okunguyena ozale uNandi unina kaShaka. Yingakho- ke ngithi isizwe sas~Lan~eni ~ibaluleke kakhulu emlandweni wakwaZulu, owakhlwa yilona iLembe. . 
  Nguyena futhi uShaka owahlasela wachitha ubukhoSI baseLangeni. Lapho ezalwa khona. Bathi n~esikhathi uShaka ebulala abantu baseLangeni wake wamshlya uMakhedam~ waze wathi akakhe umuzi waseZulwini, eduze naseNtembem. Kodwa kwathi emva kwalokho uShaka wabuye wambulala 
uMakhedama. 
  Kasazi ukuthi kwase kwenzenjani. Kuthiwa uShaka wakha umuzi wakhe lapho wawuqamba igama elithi kuseNdlamathe. Bahlakazeka abantu baseLangeni ekufeni kukaMakhedama. 
66 
UMakhedama wafa engenayo indlalifa. Empeleni yena 10 Makhedama ubukhosi kwakungesibo obakhe kodwa umfowabo omdala awumthandanga umhlaba ngoba wayeyisishaywa (enobuso obumhlophe). Yingakho nje uMakhedama athatha ubukhosi emva kokuba ekade edukele kwelaseButhonga. Yikho athola igama lokuthi iNjomane eyaduka inJinyakanyaka. 
  Bahlakazeka abantu baseLangeni. Sekuzothi ngesikhathi sokubusa kweNkosi uMpande, uSikhonyana indodana kaLuhleko kaSongweni esebuthweni leSangqu wathandana nentombi engakajutshwa. Ngokwesaba ukuthi uzobulawa wabaleka nentombazana leyo weqa uThukela, wayokhonza kwabamhlophe. Kuthe eqa nje uThukela, wabanjwa yizikawoti zikahulumeni wabamhlophe. Isigwebo sakhe kwaba ukuthi asebenze lapho inJinyaka eInithathu. Ngesikhathi esebenza lapho kwaDukuza, watholana noJantoni (John Dunn) ababa ngabangani abakhulu, kuthe uma uJantoni esekhonza enkosini yakwaZulu okwase kunguCetshwayo ngaleso sikhathi. uSikhonyane wahamba naye umngani wakhe. UJantoni wabekwa waba ngesinye seziphakanyiswa zenkosi uCetshwayo futhi wathola nokuba ngumeluleki wenkosi.

MANQONDO (MAZWANA) 
bavikeleke ezitheni babekwazi ukubona engakababoni. 
  Lokhu babekwenzela ukuba babone ukuthi isivakashi sabo ngesifanele ukwemukelwa nokuthi kufanele semukelwe kanjani, kodwa uma kuyisivakashi okungafanele semukelwe babezihlalela emgedeni wabo size sidikibale sihambe. BangaMaNtungwa-Nguni. 
  Kuthiwa abantu ababakhelene nabo baqale bacabanga ukuthi ngaBathwa ngoba bebona indlela abaphila ngayo, lena phela yokuhIala emgedeni. Ngakho abantu abaningi bazama ukukhipha Iaba bantu emgedeni ukuze bababone ukuthi bangobani, bayini. Sizwa ukuthi kwake kosiwa nenyama kucatshangelwa ukuthi uma kungaBathwa bazophuma emgedeni bekhishwa wusi. Kodwa Iutho. Kodwa ekugcineni baphuma batholakala ukuthi ngabantu abafana nabo bonke nje abantu. Kwase kufanele-ke baphumele eshashalazini njengabo bonke, baphume emgedeni. 
  Ake sibheke impilo yabo Iaba bantu behlezi Iaphaya emgedeni. Kuthiwa impilo yabo kwakungeyokuziphephisa. Lokhu ngikusho ngoba kwasithakazelo sabo sisuselwa empilweni yabo. Babelima Iaba bantu, kodwa ngokwesaba izimpi, babengenaso isikhathi esanele sokunaka amasimu abo. Kasizwa Iutho ngokufuya kwabo. Esikuzwayo ukuthi babephuma ebusuku bayosenga noma ngekabani inkomo. 
  Ngalokho babehiala namagula agcwele ubisi Iwezinkomo ezingesizo ezamaQungebe. Ngakho kwakuthi noma amagula esenamasi kodwa kunele kungafika ubisi oIusha kuqungwe ngalo. Yingakho baze babizwa ngokuthi amaQungebe nje ngoba bequnga amasi ngobisi. 
  Abantu bakwaNgobese babaluleke ngesikhathi kubusa inkosi uMpande owayebusa kwaZulu ngaleso sikhathi, kanti owayesengumholi wabantu bakwaNgobese ngaleso sikhathi kwakunguMfokazana, indodana kaXongo. UMfokazana lona wakhombisa ubuqhawe ezimpini zenkosi kangangokuthi .yaze yambonga ngokumsikela indawo esuka phezu koMzinyathi kudlule ngaphansi kweNquthu. Ngakho-ke wakwazi 
 zabo. Endaweni ababehlala noma ngumuphi umuntu ozayo 
kuyo vena 
USikhonyana waba ngenye yezinduna zikaJantoni. 
Ekuxabaneni kukaCetshwayo namaNgisi, nokuhIubuka kukaJantoni enkosini yamaZulu, kwenza ukuthi uSikhonyana anikwe indawo yaseNduIinde ukuba abuse kuyo. Emveni kwakhe kwabusa. indodana yakhe uNkomindle, vena owalandelwa nguMthengeni uyise wenkosi ebusayo manje (1993). 
AbakwaMagwaza 
Kuthe ngesikhathi sikaMakhedama kwadaleka imbedumehlwana esizweni saseLangeni. Kwakukhona indlu encane yaseLangeni kaQumbumbethe kaLugoloza. 
  Kule ndlu kwakukhona indodakazi kaMazwana, yathathwa nguMakhedama wayenza uNkosikazi Iokhu okwakungavumelekile ngokwesiko lesiNguni. Ngakho-ke ngenxa yalesi sehlo abantu bakaQumbumbethe baziwa njengabantu bakwaMagwazwa ngoba begwazwe yindoda, yasekhaya. Kwathi abantu bakaSoyingwase kwathiwa abakwaMhlongo belandela igama IikaBhebhe. 
  Ngokolimi IwesiNguni Iokugwinya amanye amagama noma izinhlamvu abantu bakaQumbumbethe kuthi ngabakwaMagwaza, kwayekwa ukuthi ngabakaMagwazwa. Le nkosazana yezimanga kwakunguSozidade, kaMazwana. Ake sibelamanise nabo Iaba bendlu encane yaseLangeni. 
AmaQungebe (Ngobese) 
AmaQungebe noma sithi abantu bakwaNgobese sibathola Iaphaya eduze kweNhlazatshe egqunyaneni eIibizwa ngokuthi kuseNtabantuzuma. Kuthiwa babehlala emgedeni ukuze

tITHATIlEZAKHE (OBUSAYO 1993) 
  Indodana kaSihayo uMehlokazulu yena wafa ngesikhathi sempi kaBhambatha kaMancinza wakwaZondi.

AbakwaZungu 
Abantu bakwaZungu sengathi YIslzwe esidala lapha ngoba sizokhumbula ukuthi uNdlunkulu kaMalandela uNozinja wayengowozalo lwalesi sibongo. Nguyena phela uNozinja ozale oQwabe noZulu. Abanye bathi abantu bakwaZungu bangamaNtungwa Nguni kanti abanye bathi bangaBambo Nguni. Kodwa sigcina ngokuthi bangaBentungwa. Lokhu sikusho ngoba bonke abahlobene nabo bangaMantungwa. 
  Ngesikhathi sikaNcwane sithola abantu bakwaZungu bakhe emagqumeni akwaillophekhulu, kuze kuyofika ezinkalweni zasOlundi. Yilapho futhi uNcwane ashonela khona. Ekushoneni kukaNcwane, washiya amadodana amabili angoMakhoba kanye noZungu. Omdala kwakunguMakhoba. Nguyena okwakufanele athathe isikhundla sikayise ekukhothameni kwakhe, kodwa ngenxa yokukhombisa izimpawu zobuthakathaka, uyise washiya ekhombe uZungu ukuthi nguyena oyothatha ubukhosi. Bathi uMakhoba wakwemukela lokhu ngokukhulu ukuzithoba. Asazi noma naye wayezibona ukuthi akafanele ukuba yiNkosi, noma wathanda kakhulu ukuthula. 
Bathi uMakhoba into ayenza wathatha abalandell bakhe 
	wayokwakha kwaNtabankulu 	kushone ngaseMfolozi 
	emnyama, kuze kuyoshaya 	eMbekamuzi. Ngalokhu 
ukwehlukana kwazalwa izizwe ezimbili esakwaMakhoba kanye nesakwaZungu. Ngesikhathi sikaShaka kwase kubusa uManzini kwaZungu. Njengoba sike sasho ngaphambilini sathi indlu kaMakhoba yathanda ukuba buthakathaka, kwenzeka ukuba bagwinywe indlu encane kaZungu. Yingakho kwathi ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaManzini abantu bakwaZungu base benabe baze bafika eMfolozi emnyama. Ngokunjalo kwasho

61. 
ukuthi umngcele wezwe lakwaZungu sekuyisizwe sakwaNdwandwe sikaZwide kaLanga, lSlZWe esasisikhulu ngaleyo nkathi. Ukuba kule ndawo kwabantu bakwaZungu kwasifaka kobukhulu ubucayi. Kuyakhumbuleka ukuthi ukushudulisana kwezindlovu ezimbili kubulala utshani. 
  Kwathi sekuqubulana uShaka noZwide, isizwe sakwaZungu sona naso sathinteka ngoba sase singumgoga okwakufanele inkosi esheshayo iwusebenzise ukuze ikwazi ukuhlasela Ie enye inkosi eyisitha sayo. Kwenzeka njalo-ke nakuManzini. Inkosi eyashesha ukukubona ukuthi uManzini kufanele asetshenziswe ngandlela thize kwaba nguShaka. Sithola ukuthi weza kuManzini ezomheha ngezinkomo, ngoba kwakutholakala ukuthi uManzini wayezifela ngezinkomo. 
  UShaka yena wayethi noma ezithanda izinkomo kodwa okwakhe okukhulu kwakungukwandisa umbuso wakhe. Ngakho wabona amabutho kaManzini ayesemancane ezihlalele nje engenzi lutho, ibutho alithanda kakhulu kwakuyibutho 
	okwakuthiwa 	ngaMankentshane. 	Ngakho-ke. uShaka 
	wakhuluma 	noManzini wathi 	akamboleke ibutho 
laManketshane yena uzomnika izinkomo. UManzini wavumela 
	phezulu wamnika uShaka ibutho. 	. 
  UManzini wayengazi ukuthi unikela ngamabutho akhe nJe kuShaka naye uyogcina esezinikele kuShaka ebalekela ulaka lukaZwide. Phela kuthe esazihlalele emzini wakhe kwaPhungambi, kwafika kuye isigijirni sivela komunye umakhelwane wakhe oyiNkosi manje yakwaNdwandwe uZwide umfokaLanga. Umlayezo kwakungowokuheha uManzini ukuba azenze isihlobo esikhulu sabantu bakwaNdwandwe. Ngamanye amagama wayecelwa ukuba abantu bakhe uZwide, nabantu bakwaZungu bakhe obukhulu ubuhlobo. Bazokwenza kanjani lokhu na? 
  UZwide njengendoda eyayihlakaniphile futhi inamaqhinga amaningi warnfunda masinyane uManzini ukuthi indoda elungile futhi engayithandi inxushunxushu, ngakho wathi kuye kababe nejadu elikhulu lezintombi zezizwe zombili ezakwaZungu nezakwaNdwandwe.   UManzini engaboni ubuqili benyoka emnyonyobelayo. wavumela phezulu, walithokozela leli su elihle kangaka elivezwa yile ndoda lobudlelwane, futhi lithinta kakhulu ekwendiselaneni. Abukho ubuhlobo obuqine ngaphezu kwalobo. Okunye okumnandi yikuthi nguZwide luqobo owayezokwenza amalungiselelo aleli jadu mbumbulu. Akuzange kumethuse uManzini ukuthi yini pho leli jadu lizokwenzelwa kwakhe? Akalenzi ngani kweminye yemizi yakhe emikhulu, njengakwaNongoma noma kwaDiovunga. 
  Okunye uManzini ayesekulibele ukuthi uyise omncane uMjiza owayembambele ebukhosini ngoba uyise akhothama esemncane, ngesikhathi sekufanele ayeke ebukhosini adedele yena, kwaba lunama, kangangokuthi isizwe saze sarnkhipha sona uqobo. Wabaleka-ke uMjiza wayokhosela kuZwide. Okusobala ukuthi wafike washo zonke izinto ezimbi ngoManzini kanye nesizwe sonke sakwaZungu. Lokhu uManzini uzokubona rnhla wejadu, ngesikhathi esebona ukuthi kukhona noMjiza kulaba bantu bakwaNdwandwe. 
  Yaqala lapho ukulusola uhlamvu impangele. Ukufika kukaMjiza nokuba mdibi ndawonye nabantu bakwaNdwandwe kwamsiza uManzini, ngoba kwamenza avuke emaqandeni. Kwafanele athi nyawo zami ngibelethe, engakabonwa ngumuntu futhi kunganake muntu. UManzini wayesazi ngawo wonke amakhanda amakhosi asahlobisa ilawu likaNtombazi unina kaZwide. Ngisho nekhanda lomakhelwane, inkosi yaseMatshalini uMlotha likwaNtombazi. Ingani nelenkosi eyayidume kakhulu ngaleso sikhathi uDingiswayo kaJobe inkosi yakwaMthethwa, lalilaphaya kwaDiovunga? Pho yena angasinda kanjani kulesi silwane esesabekayo? Kwathi kusemnandi kunjeyaya, uZwide esalokhu ebuza kuManzini ukuthi zinjani izintombi.

AbakwaNgcobo 

Abantu bakwaNgcobo bangaMalala avela eNyakatho nezwe. Lokhu ngikususela ekutheni, abantu bakwaNgcobo bahlobene kakhulu nabantu bakwaMthethwa okuyibona esazi kahle ukuthi bangaMalala. Abanye baze bathi abakwaNgcobo nabakwaMthethwa bayazalana kodwa behlukana ngezindlu kuphela. Abantu bakwaNgcobo yibona abakwazi ukwehlukanisa izindlu zabo njengoba kubaluleke kuso sonke isiNguni. Sibathola benendlunkulu, iqadi kanye nekhohlwa kuze kufike nakwisizinda. Izindlu zakwaNgcobo zikwazi ukwehlukaniseka kalula. 
Ukudabuka kwabo 

Njengoba ngishilo ukuthi sengathi baqhamuka eNyakatho nezwe ngaseButhonga, futhi isizwe abahlobene naso kakhulu isizwe sakwaMthethwa. Lokho kubenza sithi bangaMalala. Kuthiwa umuntu wokuqala owaba yinzalabantu. simthola akhe umuzi wakhe eduze komfula uThukela, ezansi nalo. Kasizwa kakhulu ngalo mnumzane. Kodwa igama lakhe kuthiwa nguVumezitha. 
	UVumezitha wazala amadodana amaningi, 	kodwa 

esizowabalula lapha ngoba ayezalwa ngunina oyedwa kwaba nguNgcobo kanye noMkheshana. Yibona nenzalo yabo esizogxila kubo uma sikhuluma ngabantu bakwaNgcobo, ngoba eziningi izibongo ezithintene noNgcobo zivela kulaba bantu ababili, abangamadodana kaVumezitha. Noma phela singeke sisho ukuthi abantwana bakaMkheshana ngabakwaNgcobo, kodwa bayazalana noma ngithi yizelamani. 
  Ukuze izinto zihambe kahle kufanele sizicaze kahle izindlu zakwaNgcobo, kusukela endlunkulu yakhona size sifike endlini encane. Kodwa sizoqala ngokuzalana kwabantu bakwaNgcobo kungakabi ngabantu bakwaNgcob!l. Kusuka kuVumezitha, kwehle njalo. Sizoqala ngezindlu ukulandelana kwazo kuze kufike kwezihlobene nazo. okuthi noma sebethathana kodwa imvelaphi yabo ibe iyinye. Phela nizokhumbula ukuthi izibongo imvamisa yazo ivela emagameni abantu. noma ezehlakalweni ezithize.

AbakwaNyuswa 
Lena yindlu enkulu yiNkumbemfece. Lokhu 

76 





kanjani, ngoba kuvela kwenye yamadoda akwaNyuswa lokhu kweNkumbemfece. Abantu bakwaNyuswa kuthiwa babakhe eduze komfula obizwa ngokuthi iMamba. ongumngenela woThukela. Kuzokhumbuleka futhi ukuthi sithe umuntu oyinzalabantu kwaNgcobo wayakhe eduze koThukela. Yingakho nendiu enkulu yakhe siyithola eduze kwalo uThukela. 
  Indiu yakwaNyuswa isukela kuVumezitha uqobo. ozale uNgcobo kanye nomnawakhe uMkheshane. UNgcobo yena uzale uDingile. uDingiIe uzale amadodana amabili, oNyuswa kanye noZonca. UNyuswa yena uzale uYemesi, kwathi uZonca yena wazala uMaguya. Kuthiwa uYemesi katholanga mntwana noma ngithi akabanga nayo indialifa kwase kuthi uMaguya, wasendlini encane wangena umkaYemesi ukuze amzalele indialifa. Nempela wazala uMbhele, yena wazala uMapholoba wodumo IwakwaNgcobo. UMapholoba uzale amadodana amathathu oSihayo (inkosima), noMavela (ikhohlwa), kanye noMgabi. Lawa kwakungamadodana kaMapholoba, ngezindlu zawo. 
 ~ USihayo uzale uDubuyana yena ozale uDeliweyo, yena wazala uMqedi namanye amakhosi. Kanti uMavela uzale amadodana amabili uMkhalelwa kanye noSinqiIa. UMkhalelwa yena uzale uDikwayo yena wazala uSotobe. Kanti uMgabi. yena uzale uNcume. yena wazala amadodana amabili oMshiswa noMnkwantshi. Ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaShaka kwaZulu, kwaNyuswa kwakubusa uMapholoba. Bathi noma izinsuku zase zihambiIe, insizwa endala yayingayishiyi ediamabele. Ngoba sithola lapha uMapholoba eseganwa ngudadewabo kaZihlandlo wasEmbo. 
  Kodwa okubi akwenza uMapholoba ukuqhatha amadodana akhe uSihayo noMgabi ethi kababange ubukhosi. Nempela babanga ngesikhathi engasekho uyise. Izindiu zonke zavuna uSihayo njengenkosana. Wasuka 10 mbango waba mkhulu kabi waze walanyulwa nguShaka. 
  Kanti kuzothi emva kwesikhathi uMgabi aqhathe uSihayo noShaka ngokuqamba amanga okuthi uSihayo uthumelele uShaka ugwayi onobuthi ukuze uma uShaka ethi

Uzalo lwabakwa Ngongoma 
uyawubhema akhothame. UShaka wakuzwa lokhu wahlasela elakwaNyuswa. Wayezoshaya aqothe imbokodo nesisekelo ukuba umhlobo wakh~ uZihlandlo kabafihlanga kuye abanye abantu bakwaNyuswa. Laba bantu bakwaNyuswa bahlala kwaze kwathi ngokuhlaselwa kukaZihlandlo nguDingane, babaleka bawelauThukela, futhi bayokwakha enhla noMhlathuzana, behambisana nabaMbo nabo ababebalekela ulaka lukaDingane. Kuthe sekuphethe urnbuso wamaNgisi. uSomtsewu (Sir Theophilus Shepstone) abantu bakwaNyuswa bakhiswa endaweni entsha enhla neMona eNdwedwe lapho beiholakala khona kuze kube namhlanje. Kodwa abakaMgabi babaleka nabo baze bafika ngaseMzimkhulu, sebephethwe yindodana kaNcurne uMshiswa. Iyona ebusa la maNyuswa aseZingolweni. 
  Kwathi enye indodana kaNeume enguMkwantshi yona yayokwakha endaweni esibizwa ngokuthi kuseMkhambathini (Carnperdown) kanye nakwaBhota (Bothas Hill). Ehlukana kanjalo-ke amaNyuswa, kodwa ebevela ndawonye. Umuzi omkhulu lapho kuzalwa khona uSihayo kwathiwa kuseNkumbini. Ngalokho uSihayo wazibiza ngeNkumbemfeee. Ukwehlukanisa uNyuswa kaSihayo nabanye oNyuswa, bayaye babizwe ngeNkumbemfeee. 
AbakwaNgongoma 
Sizokhurnbula ukuthi ngesikhathi siqala ukukhuluma ngabantu bakwaNgeobo sithe bona behlukaniswa kahle ngezindlu zabo. Kade siqeda ukukhulurna ngoNyuswa sathi indlu enkulu. Indlu yesibili kuba yikhohlwa. Ikhohlwa kaliyizali inkosana kodwa lizala iphosa kubusa. 
  Abantu bakwaNgongoma kasiqondi ukuthi kuze kuthiwe ngabakwaNgongoma nje kwakwenze njani? Bona bayasisho isigarneko, kodwa akukhona okwethu ukusibhala lapha. Okwethu ukukhulurna ngezindlu zakwaNgeobo nokwehlukana kwazo. Laba bantu bayatholakala laphaya eMsunduze eNdwedwe.

65. 
Ekuxabaneni kwabo uXhonxo wasuka wayokwakha esizweni sakwaNgubane eMdlovana (Greytown) ngasendaweni eyaziwa ngokuthi kuseHlimbithwa. Kukule ndawo lapho uXhonxo azalela khona indodana yakhe uSanimuse yena wazala uMdunane. kanti yena wazala uDindi. yena wazala uSokebi, yena wazala uDiomo. yena wazala uNonyanda yena ozale uMahawule. yena ozale amadodana amane oMavuso. Gewuka. Gintwa kanye noMadlenya. UMadlenya uzale uHhemuhhemu. okunguyena owasuka wayokwakha eMgungundlovu (Elandskop). emva kokunyakaziswa kakhulu yiLembe. UHhemuhhemu uzale uLangalakhe. 
AMaqadi 
Lena yindlu yakwaNgcobo ebalulekile ngoba phela sizokhumbula ukuthi kade sikhuluma ngekhohlwa. kanti ngaphambilini sikhulume ngendlwenkulu yakwaNyuswa. Manje sesizokhuluma ngeQadi lakwaNgcobo. Umbuzo uzothi yin! yona iQadi? Phela kuyaye kuthi uma umnurnzane esethathe indlunkulu. ebese eganwa ngunkosikazi~ wesibili. Lowo-ke uyimbangi yasendlunkulu. okusho ukuthi ngeke angene nangephutha endlunkulu. Nendodana yakhe iyoba yiphosakubusa. Okusho ukuthi iyosithola isikhundla sobukhosana uma endlunkulu engatholakalanga umfana. noma uma UInnumzane engaganwanga futhi. Kodwa uma umnumzane ebuye wathatha futhi, iphosakubusa ngeke libuse. Lo nkosikazi wesithathu yena usezofakwa endlunkulu. abe yindodakazi yakhona. Ngakho-ke uba yindlu yangakwesokudla. 
  Le ndlu njengoba sishilo sathi ingeniswe undlunkulu. uma kwenzeka inkosikazi enkulu ingamtholi umfana oyoba yindlalifa yomnumzane. kuye kuthathwe umfana wale ndlu avale isikhala. Ngakho Ie ndlu yaziwa ngokuthi iQadi. KwaNgcobo kukhona-ke isizwe esizibiza ngokuthi ngaMaqadi. Sekunesizwe saseMaqadini. nezwe laseMaqadini. AMaqadi avela nawo kuVumezitha ozale uNgcobo. ozale uDingile. yena 
80 
ozale uNyuswa noZonca kanye noNgothoma. KukuNgothoma lapha kuvela khona aMaqadi. 
  UNgothoma uzale uNjila. yena wazala uSilwane. yena wazala uDube. ye~a wazala uDabeka. yena ozale uMqhawe. ozale uMandlakaYlse. ozale uMzonjani. obusayo njengamanje (1993). La~ho aMaqadi ayakhe khona kuseZiqalabeni eduze komfula. iNsunze. Bakhelene impela nabakwaNyuswa. AMaqadi enabe aze aflka eNanda kanti kukhona futhi amanye aMaqadi aseNcwadi ngase Richmond.

AbakwaWosiyana (Nzama) 
Abantu bakwaWosiyana baziwa kakhulu ngokuthi bangabantu bakwaNzama. Noma kwesinye isikhathi ngenxa yokwehlukana kwezindawo nezigodi kuyaye kuthiwe ngabakwaZama, bamyeke u-N ekuqaleni. Kodwa lokhu akubehl';lkanisi abant~ bakwaWosiyana. Imvelaphi yabantu bakwaWoslyana sengathl iqhamuka kubantu bakwaNgcobo. Kodwa sengathi bazalana kakhulu nendlu kaMkheshane (Shangase). 
  Izinkomba zonke zikhomba ukuthi uNzama okunguyena inzalabantu wayezalana noMkheshane. Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi phela uMkheshane wayengumfowabo kaNgcobo indodana kaVumezitha. 
  Okokuqala sithola abakwaWosiyana bakhelene noNyuswa laphaya ernfudlaneni iNtolwane ongumngenela weNsuze. Okuthe ekwehlukaneni kwabakwaNyuswa nabakwaShangase ngokuxabana okuthize, ngesikhathi besuka oThukela 
86 
beyokwakha eMandlalathi, abakwaWosiyana bahamba nabo. AMandlalathi ngumfula ongumngenela woThukela ezansi nalo ngaseKranskop. Kuthe uShaka eseshakazisa izwe abantu bakwaWosiyana basuka lapho babakhe khona ngokubalekela ulaka lukaShaka bayokwakha ngaseLovu, kodwa kabazinzanga lapho. Babuye babuyela emuva bayokwakha enhla noMdloti. Yilapho imvamisa besatholakala khona. Bahamba nje nabakwaShangase bakhona lapha. 
  Njengoba namanje bakhelene. Okusakhombisa khona ukuthi banobuhlobo obukhulu, bokuzalana. Emlandweni wakwaZulu ikakhulukazi ngesikhathi kusabusa in kosi uShaka, abantu noma ngithi isibongo sakwa Wosiyana sake sathi ukugqama ngenxa yeqhawe lakhona elakhombisa esikhulu 
isibindi ngokugagamela umuzi weLembe. 	Lowo

yakwaWosiyana njengoba abanye bebesho, kodwa uGcugcwa wayeyindoda nje efana namanye amadoda esizwe. Kodwa indaba yobuqhawe bakhe izovela ngesigameko esehlela abantu bakwaWosiyana. Kuthiwa abantu bakaNzama kwakungabantu abakwazi ukuncibilikisa insimbi bakhe ngayo imikhonto kanye namakhuba okulima. 
  Sengathi lokhu kwaze kwafika nasezindlebeni zikaShaka ukuthi abantu bakwaWosiyana bayizinyanga zensimbi. UShaka njengomuntu owayematasatasa ngokwakha amabutho akhe azohlasela ngawo ngesikhathi ebumba isizwe, wacela inkosi yakwaWosiyana ukuba imakhele imithango yemikhonto. Yena (uShaka) uyokhokha ngezinkomo. Bathi kwaba ziwombe eziningi bezakha izikhali bezithumela kuShaka, kodwa ehluleke ukugcina isethembiso. Kwaze kwayiphatha kabi inkosi yakwaWosiyana, ukubona abantu bayo besebenzela ize leze. Futhi ibona ukuthi uShaka kaqonde khona ukuthi kube khona ubudlelwane kodwa uqonde iIiipi. Phol Kuzokwenziwa njani? Inkosi yafuna ikhambi ngokuba iqoqe sonke isizwe sayo ukuba kuzobhungwa ngalolu daba. Sengathi inkosi eyayibusa ngaleso sikhathi kwakunguMvakela kaKhumalo kaManjanja kaNzama. Bahamba njalo baze bayofika ernfuleni obizwa ngokuthi yiNseleni. Ekuzinzeni kwabo lapho eNseleni. bahlangana nabahlobo babo okudshe basuka nabo endaweni eyodwa eNyakatho, labo ngabantu bakwaMbokazi.

Kodwa okwesibili akubanga kuhle, ngoba uShaka sengathi wathumela kuSigotha owayebusa ngaleso sikhathi. Kuthiwa uShaka wacela izinkomo, efuna ukuba bakhombise ukuthi bakhonzile yini kuye. Kuthiwa inkosi yakwaMbonambi yayisa kuShaka izimanzi ezizadle. Wathukuthela wagana unwabu uShaka. Wakhuza umhlolo uShaka wathi ngilinina yini ukuba nginikwe izinkomazi ezizacile. 
Wafuna ukuba abantu bakwaMbonambi bayojeziswa. 
Kodwa uNqoboka owayeyinkosi yakwaSokhulu lSlzwe esakhelene nabakwaMbonambi. ngenxa yokuthi yayingumngani omkhulu kaShaka wezwa ukuthi intukuthelo kaShaka ingakanani. Wahamba wayobaxwayisa abantu bakwaMbonambi ngolaka lukaShaka. Wathatha indodana kaSigotha uMkhosana wayoyifihla. USigotha nabanye babulawa nguShaka, kodwa uMkhosana wasinda ngenxa kaNqoboka. Abanye abantu bakwaMbonambi ababehlakazekile babuya ngoba sekukhothame uShaka. Abantu bakwaMbonambi basakhe khona endaweni yabo kuze kube manje. 
Ngoba udle umfazi umkaXubuzela, WadI'uNondumo kaDonda kaShiya, Wadl'uMangxangxa kaDonda kaShiya, wadl'uValeIisani khona kwaShiya, Wadl'uMlovu kaNgogwana khona kwaShiya. Silo singalelwa kubakhwekazi, Ngokushis'izindlu zabakhwekazi.

71. 
AbakwaDube 
Abantu bakwaDube batholakala eNingizirnu yesizwe sakwaMbonambi eduze nolwandle. Kutholakala ukuthi abantu bakwaMbonambi nabakwaDube bayazalana. Indawo yabo enkulu iseduze komfula uMhlathuze, ikakhulu emngeneleni wawo uMhlathuze. . Kuthiwa ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaKhushwayo, abantu bakwaDube bazinikela embusweni kaDingiswayo, kwaze kwathi noma sekubusa uShaka bazinikela kuye ukuze baphephe. Lokho kwenza ukuthi noma sekubusa uNzwakele, kodwa isizwe sakwaDube sasisakhosele 
ephikweni likaShaka. 
  Abantu bakwaDube baqale ukuba nenkinga ngesikhathi sokukhothama kwenkosi uShaka, lapho inkosi uDingane waqala khona ukuzingela bonke abantu abayizihlobo zikaShaka. Sizokhumbula ebulala uNqetho wakwaKhuzwayo, simkhumbule futhi ehlasela uZihlandlo wakwaMkhize kanye noDube waseMaqadini. Nokubaleka kwabantu bakwaCele, uMningi owabuya wayesakha umuzi waseMandlanzini, kwaze kwavela isizwe saseMandlazini, noNzwakele wangena kulolo zungu lukaDingane, wabulawa nguye uDingane. Kwase kungukuqala kwalo usizi lwabantu bakwaDube. Ngoba baphoqeka ukushiya izwe labo bawele uThukela, babe yimihambuma. 
Kwathi uma uDingane esefuna ukubulala aqede abantu 
bakwaDube, ngenhlanhla eduze kwesizwe sakwaDube kwakukhona uNqoboka wakwaSokhulu, owanele wakuzwa lokhu wase ethatha omunye wondlunkulu bakaNzwakele owayekhulelwe wayomfihla kwakhe. Kwathi ekufeni kukaNzwakele umkakhe wathola umfana uHabane, okunguyena owaqhuba ulibo Iwabantu bakwaDube. UNqoboka kwakungomunye wezihlobo zikaShak~ owayesenqamukile ukuvakashela kwaZulu ngoba umngam wakhe uShaka wayesekhotheme, sekubusa isitha sakhe uDingane. Kuthe ukuba uDingane ehlulwe ng~Mpande, wabaleka waze wayofela ezintabeni zoBombo. Ufa nJe abantu bakwaDube wabahlakaza bagcwala izintaba. Iqoqwana labo 
98 
lalakhe laphaya ngaphesheya koThukela kwaMandelu, eNyakatho nomfula uMvoti. 
  Ekufeni kukaNzwakele uDingane wathatha umngani wakhe wakwaZungu obizo lakhe linguMadlebe, indodana kaMgedeza, owayakhe eMpaphala ngaseNtumeni eShowe, Wabuye wathumela enye indoda yakwaZungu ukuba izoba yiso lakhe elibheke 10 Madlebe, ukuthi ulibheke kahle yini izwe lakwaDube, uDingane ayeselidlile, Lo kwakunguMahuhulo waseMahlabathini. UMahuhulo wabulawa nguMpande. Kwathi izinto sezimi kahle kubusa uMpande kwezwakala ukuthi uNqoboka ufihle inkonyane kaNzwakele. La mahebezi ayezwiwe ngumntwana uCetshwayo, ngoba ezwa ukuthi uHabane ucishe wabulawa yinyathi kuzingelwa, wasinda ngokuba ala Ie phansi. yase imdovadova ngezinyawo. 
  Bacela ukuba uNqoboka alethe uHabane kubo, uma ngithi kubo ngiqonde inkosi uMpande kanye nomntwana uCetshwayo. Walethwa-ke ngempela uHabane, wemukelwa kahle, kwathiwa akayokwakha endaweni yakwaDube, kodwa yena kathandanga, wafuna ukuyozihlanganisa nabantu bakubo ngaphesheya koThukela, kwaMandelu.

  Ngale mpumelelo yakhe uNqoboka, kwafanele ahambe ayobonga kumsizi wakhe onguDingiswayo. Kulapho ekuvakasheni kwakhe kwaMthethwa lapho uShaka ambona khona kwathi noma uNqoboka emdala kunaye kodwa wamthanda.   Kuthiwa kwathi esemdala kwaba nombango emadodaneni, uNontsobo kanye noGcabashe wehlulwa uGcabashe wabulawa. Kodwa uNqoboka akumphathanga kahle lokhu, kangangokuthi wabuye waphakamisa uMaphumane ukuba abangise uNontsobo. Wehlulwa futhi uMaphumane wabalekela ngaphesheya koThukela. Bathi uNqoboka wafa esegodukiswa yinceku yakhe ngokubonisana nendodana.

kaMdolomba. Kuthiwa uViiana waba ngezinye zezinsika zomuzi kaDingiswayo owawubizwa ngokuthi kusoHheni. Okwathi emva kwesikhathi waba yinduna. 
  Ngokuthi wake waba yinsila yenkosi, kwabe sekuthiwa abantu bakwaMkhwanazi ngoNkwali yenkosi, behlonipha insila yenkosi. Abantu bakwaMkhwanazi kwase kuthiwa ngabeZembe. UMalanda indodana kaViiana waganiselwa nguMpande udadewabo uNtikili ozale uSomkhele uyise kaMtubatuba. Yingakho nje kukhona idolobha laseMtubatuba ezweni lakwaMpukunyoni, kulandela igama likaMtubatuba. 
  Abantu bakwaMpukunyoni (bakwaMkhwanazi) basakhile kuleya ndawo yabo ngaphansi kwenkosi uMinias Mkhwanazi (1993). Kwathi indodana kaMdinwa, uPhalane wanikwa indawo yakwaDlangezwa nguCetshwayo. UPhalane uzale uNgogwane, yena ozale uMntongenakudla, yen a ozale inkosi ebusayo njengamanje (1993).

AbakwaMpukunyoni (Mkhwanazi)
