oNdlovu nokuthiwa ngoMotioung noma okuthiwa ngoTiou. Kodwa iqiniso lithi abantu bakwaNdlovu badabuka endaweni yaseNkandla, bayingxenye yesizwe saMachunu. Abantu esikhuluma ngabo lapha, ngabantu bakaMpongo, kaZingelwayo kaLamula kaGatsheni. Laba bantu bakwaNdlovu bakhelene nabantu bakaMavovo wakwaMkhize phezu komfula iNsuze ngaphansi kwaseQhudeni eNkandla. Okwathi ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaMadngwane eMachunwini, kwaba khona ukungezwani phakathi kukaMpongo nenkosi yaseMachunwini, bethi uMpongo uyathakatha ngoba wayefuye izinyoni ezimbili ezithi kazifane nokhozi. Babaleka abantu bakwaNdlovu bayokhonza kuZihlandlo wakwaMkhize, bebalekela ulaka lukaMacingwane. 
  Kuthe lapho besathi banethezekile kwaMkhize, kwasuka inkosi yakwaZulu uDingane yahlasela uZihlandlo yambulala. Abantu bakwaMkhize behlangene nabakwaNdlovu babaleka balibhekisa ngaseNingizimu, baze bayofika egqumaneni laseNhlazuka eduze nomfula iLovu. AbakwaMkhize base beholwa yindodana kaZihlandlo uMsengi, abakwaNdlovu bona base beholwa nguNgema indo dana kaMpongo. UNgema wazala uNogwiyela, yena wazala uMdingi. UMdingi yena wasuka eNhlazuka wayokwakha eMngeni. Ngokuhlaselwa kwabo nguMacingwane baze bayokhonza kuZihlandlo, bazibona bengasenaboya. Nangokuhlaselwa kukaZihlandlo nguDingane kanti nguyena obese ebafukamele. babona ukuthi uboya babo obungamandla abo, bazibiza ngokuthi bangabakwaBoya benyathi obuthi busongwa bube busombuluka.

AbakwaMpungose 
Abantu bakwaMpungose kuthiwa baphuma kubantu bakwaGwabini. Abantu bakwaMpungose babizwa kanjena ngoba kulandelwa igama lomsunguli walesi sizwe. UMpungose lona wayevela emndenini wendlunkulu kaMalandela uNozinja unina woQwabe benoZulu. Uyise kaMpungose kwakunguPhahla. Ngenxa yokuthi uPhahla wayehlobene nondlunkulu kaMalandela, owayefike kuqala wakha kulo lonke leli laseBabanango, wakhisa uPhahla eThalaneni, ngaseNkandla. Umuzi awakha lapho wawubizwa ngokuthi kusoYengweni. Abantu bakwaMpungose babakhelene nabakwaSikhakhane kanye naMachunu. Ngesikhathi senkosi uShaka isizwe sakwaMpungose sasigcwele naseNhlazatshe, kepha lapho sasibuswa nguNdlovu indo dana kaKhuba. 
  Kungesikhathi senkosi uMpande lapho uSilwane indodana kaNdlovu anikwa khona nguMpande indawo yabantu bakwaXulu eMfule ngaseMthonjaneni, ukuba ayiphathe. Le ndawo ize iyoshaya eMfolozi emhlophe.

  Kusukela kuMnyamana abantu bakwaButhelezi bathola isikhundla sokuba ngoNdunankulu bamakhosi ayebusa uZulu ngaleso sikhathi. UMnyamana waba nguNdunankulu wenkosi 
107 

yathola umusa enkosini uMpande yona wayoyakhisa eMlalazi. ezweni okwakungelakwaQwabe. Kanti abanye basala eNkandla. Abantu bakwaMpungose banamakhosi abo. 
AbakwaButhelezi . 
Uma kukhulunywa ngendawo yaseMcakweni kanye naseMpembeni, eMaqungebeni kanye neBabanango, kukhulunywa lapho ngemingcele yezwe lakwaButhelezi. Kuthiwa isizwe sakwaButhelezi singesinye sezizwe' ezindala lapha ezweni lakwaZulu. Imvelaphi yabo sengathi iyafana neyoMalandela. AbakwaButhelezi bangaMantungwa aqhamuka enhla nezwe, yikho lokhu abanye bebethi bangabeSuthu. Kodwa iqiniso kalaziwa kahle hIe. 
	Ngesikhathi 	sikaSenzangakhona 	ebusa 	kwaZulu 
noDingiswayo ebusa kwaMthethwa, kwaButhelezi kwakubusa uPhungashe indodana kaQwangubana. Kufika esikhathini nje sikaPhungashe kade saba khona isizwe sakwaButhelezi. Umlando waso usukela kuShenge owayephila ngabo 1640. Uma ubheka yisizwe esidala lesi. uCetshwayo, uMathole waba ngumnumzane nomeluleki

	nguNdunankulu 	nomeluleki weNgonyama 
yakwaKhethomthandayo uBhekuzulu, kuze kube yile Ngonyama usenguNdunankulu. 
AmaChunu 
AmaChunu angaMantungwa Nguni njengabantu bakwaZulu, Khumalo kanye noQwabe. Lokhu sikuthathela ekutheni imvelaphi yabantu balezi zibongo iseNingizimu-Mpumalanga yeNtiiasifali. Kodwa lapho sibathola sebezinze khona ekufikeni kwabo kwelakwaZulu, kwakuphakathi kweThalaneni eNkandia kanye noMzinyathi. Kuthi omakhelwane babo ngaseMpumalanga kwakungaMabomvu kanye nabaseMbo, kanti ngaseNtshonalanga kwakungabaThembu. Okuthe ekuhlaseleni kukaShaka uMacingwane, bahlakazeka abantu bakwaMchunu abanye balishiya eIendabuko yabo kodwa abanye basala basekhona namanje kuleyo ndawo yabo. 
  Ukuqinisa ukuthi abantu baseMachunwini babakhelene nabaseMbo sizokhumbula ukuthi kwathi ngesinye isikhathi abantu baseMbo benenkosi yabo uMavovo nabaseMachunwini babenoMavovo nakhona kuze kuduka intombi yaseMabomvini eyayiyogana uMavovo waseMbo kodwa yahlangana noMavovo waseMachunwini, waseyikhohlisa intombi wathi nguyena uMavovo kodwa umakhelwane wakhe nguMavovana. Okwathi esekuzwa lokhu 10 omunye uMavovo, wahlomisa impi ukuba iyolanda Ie ntombi. 
  Ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaDingiswayo kwaMthethwa yilapho isizwe sakwaMchunu sagqama khona kuze kufike esikhathini sokubusa kweLembe, ngoba isizwe sakwaMchunu ngaleso sikhathi sabe sibuswa nguMacingwane. Umuzi kaMacingwane wawuphezu kweThala, waziwa ngokuthi kuseNgonyameni, echaza ukuthi uyinkosi enkulu ngaphezu kwawo wonke amakhosi akhelene nawo. Ngakho wayezibiza ngebhubesi loqobo. Lokhu yikho okwamfakela isigcWagcwa kuDingiswayo kanye noShaka.

76. 
  Sizokhumbula ukuthi uDingiswayo wayeqala umsebenzi wokuhlasela izizwe kodwa umuntu owayefike awuqedele lowo msebenzi nguShaka. Sizokhumbula ukuthi uMacingwane wamhlupha kanjani uMpongo wakwaNdiovu waze wabaleka wayozinikela kuZihlandlo wakwaMkhize owaze wamkhoselisa naye ethembe uShaka okwakungumhlobo wakhe. Abantu baseMachunwini bazalana nabantu bakwaNdiela, Ndima Lembede. 
  Kuhambe kwahamba abantu bakwaNdiela sekubusa uLembede baxabana nabakwaMchunu. KwaMchunu kwase kubusa uLubhoko. Baze basuka bayokwakha kwaNtabankulu ngasemthonjeni weMfolozi emnyama, besuka eSikhaleni Sebomvu. Ngesikhathi abantu bakaLembede bebalekela uLubhoko, uLembede wasala esebulewe base bebekisa ngesihlahla esithize ukuthi wangcwatshwa kuphi. Leso sihlahla kuze kube manje kuthiwa yisihlahla sikaLembede. Izibongo ezihlobene nabantu bakwaMchunu yilezi: Majola. Mcumane, Ngqulunga, Ndawonde. Abantu bakwaMchunu sebeyisizwe esikhulu laphaya eMsinga, noma zikhona izinsalelana laphaya eNkandla. 
AbakwaXulu 
Abantu bakwaXulu ayiqondakali kahle imvelaphi yabo. phakathi kwaMalala kanye naMathonga. Abanye baze bathi bavela eMaMpondweni. Kuthiwa babehlobene naBathembu baseKoloni. Kodwaabanye bathi abantu bakwaXulu bangamaNguni angamaNtungwa ngoba lapho betholakala sebezinze khona omakhelwane babo sithola kungabantu bakwaSibiya kanye nabaseLangeni. Ake sikhulume ngabantu bakwaXulu lapho sibafica bezinze khona ngaphansi kukaXabhashe. Indawo lapho sibathola khona abantu bakwaXulu babakhe phakathi komfula uMfule kanye neMfolozi eMhlophe ngokubhekela ngasolwandle. 
  Kuthiwa lesi sizwe sasizihlalele nomakhelwane baso ngokukhulu ukuthula lokhu. Kuze kwathi ngesikhathi senkosi yakwaMthethwa uDingiswayo ngoba efuna ukwakha ubukhosi 
110 
bakhe. wase ehlasela uXabhashe nesizwe sakhe. khona laphaya ngaseMthonjaneni. 
  Phela kungaleso sikhathi lapho uDingiswayo ayefuna khona ukudlondlobala abe yinkosi yomhlaba wonke. zonke izizwe ayesezinqobile zikhonze ngaphansi kwakhe. NoXabhashe-ke wawela kulolo gibe lokuthola inkosi yakwaMthethwa yomele ukuphatha ngamandla amakhulu angakaze abonwe nanini. 
  Bathi uXabhashe ngobunye ubusuku obejwayelekile wayeziialele engazeIele lutho kanti uzohlaselwa ngalobo busuku. Bathi wathi ephaphama emaphusheni akhe amnandi. waphaphama eseyisiboshwa sikaDingiswayo. ngoba impi yakwaMthethwa yahlasela ebusuku futhi kungazelele muntu, bonke abantu beIele. Kuthiwa ekuvukeni kwakhe uXabhashe wathukuthela kakhulu waze wamelwa yinhIiziyo, wafa. Kwawathukuthelisa kakhulu amaqhawe akwaXulu okwase kwehlele inkosi yabo. Bazama imizamo yokuba baphindisele kubasocongi, kodwa kwatholakala ukuthi impi kaDingiswayo inamandla kakhulu, ngakho yachithwa eyakwaXulu. Yabaleka yaze yayotheleka ezweni lakwaQwabe, ngaphesheya koMhlathuze eduze kwentaba ebizwa ngokuthi kukwaHiokohloko eduze komthombo kaKhondio. 
  UXabhashe wangcwatshwa lapho afela khona, ithuna lakhe Iiyatholakala laphaya egqumeni laseLumbi. Okwaba ngumshophi omkhulu kubantu bakwaXulu kwaba ukufa kukaTshana indodana kaXabhashe ibulawa ukugula nje. Nayo futhi yangcwatshwa laphaya eLumbi. Kusengathi kwakuyindodana yokugcina yoliba lukaXabhashe, ngoba emva kwalokho uliba Iwase luxhuma kuMapholoba indodana kaSweIi kaMgidi, kaNomandla' kaMakhathini. Kuthe ngalesi sikhathi sikaMapholoba bahlaselwa futhi nguShaka inkosi yakwaZulu. 
Nalapha abantu bakwaXulu' .Jcabazibekanga phansi. 
Yahlangana eNyana kwatholakala ukuthi abantu bakwaXulu kabakumelana nempi kaShaka eyayihlelwe kahle. Banqotshwa, kwathi uMapholoba wafeIa kwaMaqhwakazi kanye nomfowabo uMadiozi. Kwasinda umfowabo. enye yamadodana kaSweIi uNohadu. Vena wazama ukubuyela

AbakwaSikhakhane 
AbakwaSikhakhane bavele ngoSikhakha wakwaXulu. Bathi uSikhakha lona welelesa ngoba watholakala endnda odengezini olwalundnda amakhosi akwaXulu kuphela. USikhakha yena wayengesiye owendlu yasebukhosini, ngakho wayengafanele ukundnda kulolu dengezi. Lokhu kwakusho umbango. Ngakho-ke indlela yokumjezisa uSikhakha kwaba ukuthi axoshwe emndenini. Nangempela wahamba nabalandeli bakhe bayokwakha ngaseThalaneni bakhelana nabantu bakwaMpungose. Ukuze abantu bakaSikhakha babe 
112 
nomehluko kubantu bakwaXulu wathi kababonakale ngokufaka izikhakha ezirnfishane (phela isikhakha ngelinye igama elisho isidwaba). 
Abantu bebona laba bantu abafake izidwaba ezirnfishane base bethi ngabakwaSikhakhana, bethi ngabantu bezidwaba ezirnfishane.

AbakwaDiudla 
AbakwaDiudla baphuma kwaXulu basuka eMfule bayokwakha ngaseMthinemide bakhelene nabakwaMagwaza. Ngesikhathi sokubusa kwenkosi uShaka, umholi wesizwe sakwaDiudla kwakunguNtsukungaye kaMa don do waseNketheni. Abantu bakwaDiudla bafana nabantu baseMambatheni lapho kukhona amaMbatha amnyama namhlophe. 
Nabo-ke kukhona amaDludla amnyama namhlophe.

Abantu baseBathenjini 
Igama elithi Thembu, lisuselwa efithenjini, lapho umuntu eganwe khona ngamakhosikazi amaningi. Kusengathi nesizwe saBathembu savela kanjalo. Isizwe saBathembu, singesinye sezinsika zakwaZulu. ABathembu kwasendulo babakhelene naMaMbatha kanye naMachunu kanye nabakwaMabaso. Ngalokho sibathatha njengaMantungwa Nguni. Lokhu 
113 






kufakazelwa ukuthi onke aMantungwa Nguni asuka eNingizimu neNtiiasifali ehla njalo aqonda ngasogwilll lolwandle. Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi uMalandela owazala abakwaQwabe nabakwaZulu, walandela wona 10 mgudu njengegama lakhe. 
  Njengoba uMalandela ehla eqhamuka ezweni lasenhla, noMangqiyima okunguyena ongumsuka wabantu baseBathenjini wasuka khona eNingizimu yeNtiiasifali, wehla washona ngasolwandle. Kuthiwa baze bayozinza ngaphezu komfula iNseleni, ihlalankosi lakhona kwakuthiwa kuseNhlangwini. Yilapho nangesikhathi sikaDingiswayo inkosi yakwaMthethwa yahlasela khona uJama indodana kaMnisi owayebusa aBathembu ngaleso sikhathi. 
  Okwathi ekufeni kwakhe ubukhosi baBathembu obase buwubukhosi obungelutho, bathathwa nguNdina naVe oyindodana kaMnisi, kodwa owabusa njengenduna kaDingiswayo owayeselinqobile elaBathembu. Okwabuye kwashabalalisa ithemba 10bukl1osi baBathembu ukuthi buyobuye buvuke kwaba ukuthi ngesikhathi sokukhothama kukaDingiswayo kwathatha uShaka esikhundleni sakhe, ongabanikanga ithuba abantu baseBathenjini ukuba basimame. UVico indodana kaNdima yashiya izwe lakubo yayokwakha eMhlathuze ngoba inengwa ukuthi kayisenkosi yalutho. Ngeshwa akatholanga unmtwana owamlandela esikhundleni sobuholi baBathembu. 
  Kwathi umfowabo uSondaba wathatha ubukhosi noma babebanga nomfowabo uMngcikivana kodwa uSondaba wazala indodana yakhe uSiyembeyembe, kodwa naVe uSiyembeyembe wafa engashiyanga ndlalifa. 
  Indaba yabuyela kuJama futhi ngoba kwabuye kwathatha indo dana yakhe uMhawana waqhuba uliba lobuholi baseBathenjini, emveni kwakhe kwathatha indodana yakhe uMmangaliso, Vena owazala uLokothwayo. Sengathi ubuholi baseBathenjini babuye banyamalala futhi emva kukaLokothwayo. 
  Kwaze kwathi ngesikhathi sekubusa inkosi uMpande kwaZulu lapho athatha khona uSomopho urnzukulu kaBhacile 
114 
wamenza induna yakhe eyethembekile ukuba ikhulise indodana yakhe umntwana uCetshwayo, abe ngurneluleki wakhe futhi. Lokho kwenza ukuba indlu encane kaNdaba indJu kaBhacile kube ViVona ethatha ubuholi baseBathenjini. 
  Laba Bathembu engikhuluma ngabo lapha ngaBathembu basoGwini njengoba baziwa kanjalo. Manje ake sibheke ukuzalana kwabo noma singeke sikuqede konke.

AbaseMachubeni (Shezi) 
  Abantu baseMaehubeni badume ngokuthi bangabantu bakwaShezi, kanti umholi neqhawe lakhona elidumile nguSigananda owabulawa ngamaNgisi ngesikhathi sempi kaBhambada wakwaZondi, indodana kaMandnza. 
  Lesi sizwe sizinze laphaya eNkandla futhi sidume ngehlathi lakhona eliyisinindolo. Kanti futhi bakhe entabeni, abathi uma besho ngeyesizwe sakhona. Le ntaba igama layo kuthiwa kukwaManziphambana. Ihlathi laseNkandla njengoba laziwa kuthiwa libaluleke kakhulu emlandweni wakwaZulu ngoba uShaka ngesikhathi elwa noZwide walisebenzisa leli hlathi efihle khona izinkomo nokudla kanye nabesimame. Nalapho isihleWa ekaShaka yahlehlela kulo leli hlathi. Empeleni singasho ukuthi yilapho ayinqobela khona uShaka impi kaZwide. Okwesibili, sizokhumbula ukuthi idlinza lenkosi

uCetshwayo likuleli hlathi, futhi libhekwe yibona abantu baseMaehubeni. Okwesithathu, uBhambada wakwaZondi naye wasebenzisa lona leli hlathi ngempi yamakhanda. 
  Kuthiwa isizwe saMaehube kwakuyisizwe esasibusa ngokukhulu ukuthula, kwaze konakala ngesikhathi sokuba uBhambada abalekele khona kanti ulandelwa ngamabutho amaNgisi. Wangena esihibeni.ke uSigananda owageina eboshiwe ebekwe icala lokuvukela umbuso.

Ake sibheke ukuthi ngubani umsunguli waMaehube.

AbaseMasomini 
Abantu baseMasomini kuthiwa babengabantu noma ngithi bangumsuka wabantu bakwaQwabe. Kuthiwa enye yamadoda akwaQwabe 'yawela uThukela 'ngaphambi kokuba kuwele abakwaKhuzwayo nabakwaMakhanya. 
  Sokhumbula ukuthi isibongo sakwaMakhanya sivele kubantu bakwaKhuzwayo ababotha umkhanya. Kuthiwa laba bantu babakhe ngasemsukeni womfula iNonot!, endaweni okuthiwa kuseSidumbini. Inkosi yalaba bantu kwathi ngelinye

ilanga ifuna ukubeka inkosana noma indlalifa eyobusa uma yona isikhotheme, yase yenza umncintiswano. Bathi yabulala inkomo yase iyikhipha izitho njengokujwayelekile. 
  Ikwenza konke lokhu kayitsheli muntu isu layo ngisho nezinduna zayo. Kwathi izitho sezibekiwe, yase ibiza amadodana omabili akhankasele ubukhosana. Yabe isiwacela ukuba athathe isitho ngasinye asithandayo. 
  Bathi enye indodana eyayiligovu, ifuna ukuthatha inyama eningi, yathatha umlenze. Uyise wathi kule ndodana wena uthathe umlenze, lesi yisitho eseyeka kakhulu kunezinye izitho. Lokhu kufakazela ukuba ubukhosi kawubufanele, ngokuthatha kwakho lesi sitho. Ngakho igama lakhe kwathiwa nguMeyiwa, wase ezala abantu bakwaMeyiwa. 
  Indodana yesibili, ibhekwe ngabaphansi yona yathatha ubambo. Igama layo kwakunguSingila. Uyise wathi kuSingila, uyabona wena ngoba uthathe ubambo, uthathe inyama esemqoka kuzo zonke izinyama ngoba ivikela izitho ezibucayi zibe zisemqoka empilweni yomuntu okusho ukuthi kawuhehwanga yinyama njengomfowenu kodwa uthathe ubambo olungenanyama ngoba ucabanga ukuthi lusemqoka, ngokuvikela izitho ezibucayi, okusho ukuthi uyokwazi ukuvikela isizwe esithi sintekenteke kodwa sibe sisemqoka enhliziyweni yakho. Ngakho nguwena okufanele ube yinkosi ekukhothameni kwami. Ngalokho uSingila wathatha isikhundla sikayise kwathi uMeyiwa washiya umfowabo wahamba nabantu bakhe sekungabakwaMeyiwa.

UMASENDE 

  USingila wakha umuzi wakhe phansi kwezihlahla ezazizalela izinyoni ezaziwa ngokuthi ngamasomi. Kwase kuthiwa kuseMasomini. Ngakho bonke abantu bakaSingila kwathiwa ngabaseMasomini. Kuthiwa indoda eyasuka kubo kaQwabe yayokwakha ngaphesheya koThukela kwakunguMbhedu owayaziwa ngokuthi nguNomndayi. Ngesikhathi sikaNomncayi laba bantu babengakaziwa ukuthi ngabaseMasomini. UNomndayi wazala amadodana amabili, oGwayi kanye noMoyeni. 
  Abantu bakaMbhecwa manje batholakala laphaya eMkhomazi, kafolti abakaKude bona batholakala laphaya ngaseMangangem enhla nomfula uMlazi, kanti bayatholakala eduze kweMona ngaseLumbi. 

AbaseMathulini noma AbakwaLuthuli 
Uma umuntu ebheka isihloko ngaphezulu, sisho into ebalulekile kakhulu mayelana nesibongo sakwaLuthuli. Ngenhla sikhulume ngabaseMathulini kanye nabakwaLuthuli. Ngabe zahlukene yini lezi zibongo? Noma yisibongo esisodwa? 
  Emandulo .kuthiwa abantu bakwaLuthuli babengabantu beslbongo eSlsodwa nabakwaNgcolosi, bakhelene nesizwe sakwaN?co.bo ngaseSiweni Samanqe, ngaseMpaphala e~thonJem womfula Amatigulu. Kuthiwa bangamaLala nJeng~bantu bakwaNgcobo. Kuthiwa benaba njalo baze bayoflka eNtumeni. Ngesikhathi sokubusa kwenkosi uShaka, abantu bakwaLuthuli babebuswa nguMashiza indodana kaMavela kaNkomo. 
  Kuthiwa uShaka akazange abahluphe laba bantu kodwa umuntu owaba luhlupho kakhulu kubona, kwaba yinkosi yakwaQwabe uPhakathwayo. Ngoba kusuke abaseMbedwini abazalwa kwaQwabe bathanda leya ndawo yaseMpaphala. 
  UPhakathwayo wase ehlasela abantu bakwaLuthuli ukuze Ie ~dawo ayitholele abafowabo baseMambedwini. Kuthiwa enye mdoda yakwaLuthuli yadikila yahamba yashiya abantu bakubo ngoba inengwa ukuphathwa ngabantu bakwaQwabe. Igama laleyo ndoda kwakunguShadwa kaSivuba kaDole kaMandlanduna.   Bazama ukumlandela ukuze bamephuce 10 mlalazi ngoba phela kwakuthi uma amakhosi alapha egeza noma ezisusa uthuli ezinyaweni arne kuwo 10 mlalazi osuhambe noShadwa. Kwakuthi noma befuna ukuzikhatha ngamafutha belapha izinyawo zabo (ngisho phela amakhosi akwaLuthuli) arne kuwo 10 mlalazi. Kuthiwa uShadwa wabalekela ngaseNingizimu, kwakhona abasalayo laphaya eMpaphala, besala nendodana kaMashiza uPhosula kanye nomnawakhe wasekhohlwa uMjomba, kodwa nabo laba bobabili babuye baphambana ngokukhuluma, kwathi uPhosula wabalekela umfowabo wayozinikela kuPhakathwayo inkosi yakwaQwabe. Wathi uma esehlasela umfowabo esizwa ngabakwaQwabe, wabaleka noMjomba wayokhonza kuMgabhi inkosi yaseLangeni ngaphesheya koMhlathuze. 
  UPhosula wazala uSibukeyana, yena owazala uWojiwoji, yena owazala uNjubanjuba obantu bakhe batholakala eMvoti. UShadwa owabalekela ngaseNingizimu, weqa uThukela washona ngasogwini wayofika eSibubulungu (Bluff) ngasolwandle. Wakha esinindolweni sehlathi ecashela ukuthi angabonwa muntu. Bebona ingoxo yechibi elivela olwandle belibuka besegqumaneni abalakhele, babiza leyo ndawo ngokuthi yitheku, okusho isende elilodwa. 
  Ngenxa yokuthi uShadwa wayefuna ukuzehlukanisa impela nabantu bakubo eMpaphala, futhi efuna ukuba bangawutholi umkhondo wakhe, wabiza abantu bakhe ngokuthi bangaMathuli, esikhundleni sokuthi bangabakwaLuthuli. AbakwaNgcolosi 
Abantu bakwaNgcolosi sithola ukuthi bayazalana nabantu bakwaLuthuli. Babakhe eduze nomfula Amandlalathi ngaphansi kweKranskop. Ngingasho futhi ukuthi laba bantu bangaMalala. 
  Ngesikhathi sokubusa kwenkosi uShaka babebuswa nguMmepho kaNgwane kaLamula kaNgwabini. Kuthiwa abantu bakwaNgcolosi babona abantu bakwaMchunu kanye naBathembu bebaleka bebalekela uShaka, kwathi abakwaNgcobo nabakwaMkhize bona basheshe bazinikela kuShaka. Lokhu abantu bakwaNgcolosi bakubona kungobukhulu ubuhlakani ukuzinikela. Lokho kwaba ukuziphephisa kwabo olakeni lukaShaka, bahlala ngokuthula ngaphansi kwephiko likaShaka kwaze kwaphazamiseka ukuthula kwabo ngesikhathi sekubusa uDingane owayengafuni nakuzwa nje ngabantu ababezwana noma bengabanganibakaShaka. 
  Kukhona kodwa abanye besizwe sakwaNgcolosi bona abazimbandakanya naMachunu naBathembu babaleka kanye nabo, baze bafika ezweni laMaxesibe. Kuthiwa ngesikhathi behamba laba bantu badundubala intaba uMbombo,

  Kuthiwa ngesikhathi sokubusa kwenkosi yakwaMthethwa uDingiswayo, kwaCele kwakubusa uDubandlela. Kuthiwa uDubandlela waba nenkulu inkinga ngoba bathi wahlala waze wakhula kakhulu. Amadodana akhe okwakufanele athathe ubukhosi emva kwakhe aze ashona kwawona. Endala kwakunguMdinsilwa owashona nendodana yakhe, bengabusanga. Encane kwakunguVico, naye uVico washona uyise esekhona. Kwase kuthi amadodana akhe oMande noMagaye, babanga laba bafana phambi kukayisemkhulu. Bathi uDubandlela wayenomuzi wakhe kule ndawo osekuthiwa yiGroutvilie manje. 
	Ekubangeni 	kwabazukulu 	bakhe 	uDubandlela, 
kwaphumelela uMagaye. Washiya ernzini kayisemkhulu wayokwakha owakhe umuzi emthonjeni wornfula uMhiali, kwathi umfowabo uMande yena wawela uMvoti wazokwakha lapho osekuyidolobha khona lakwaDukuza (Stanger). 
  Kwathi lezi zinsizwa zisazihlalele emizini yazo kwafika isithunywa sivela kuShaka, saqale saya kuMande, sathi uthi uShaka impi yakhe ilambile ifuna ukuba ithole ukudla ukuze ithole amandla okulwa. UMande wakhomba inja endala ezacile wathi kabathathe yona'bayokudla. Bedluia kuMande baqonda kuMagaye, bafike basho umIayezo of ana yo. UMagaye yena wathi uzobanikeza konke abakufunayo. Nangernpela wawondla amabutho enkosi yakwaZulu. UShaka ezwa indaba kaMande wathukuthela wafa. Kepha washeshe wabaleka nabantu bakhe bashiya yonke imfuyo yabo esitheni. Wabaleka wayocasha ehlathini ngasolwandle. 
UShaka wathi makangalandelwa kodwa wancishwa ukudla. 
Yabhoka indlala ehlathini kangangokuthi waze wacela umfowabo owayehlezi ngokukhulu ukunethezeka ukuba ayomncengela kuShaka. Wakwenza lokhu uMagaye. Nempela uShaka wamvumela ukuba abuyele ekhaya lakhe. Kwathi lapho esehlezi ngokukhulu ukunethezeka, safika futhi isithunywa siqhamuka kuShaka size kuMande, bethunywe nguShaka ukuba bazobulala leya nja ezacile. Kepha iqiniso ukuthi wayengasaqonde yona inja, kodwa wayeseqonde uMande uqobo. UMande wakubona lokhu, ngoba bathi wavele

wanyamalala. Kwase kuthi uShaka wavele wazikhokhisela ngokuthi akhe urnuzi wakhe emanxiweni kaMande wawuqamba ngokuthi kukwaDukuza.

AbaseMandlanzini 
Abantu baseMandlanzini, ngabantu bakwaCele. Ngesikhathi abantu bakwaCele bebalekela uDingane baze bayofika lena eMzimkhulu, abanye izinhliziyo zabo zazisasele lena emanxiweni. UMningi, enye yamadoda akwaCele, washiya isizwe sakubo waphindela emanxiweni akubo, kodwa ngoba kwakungasekho muntu kuleya ndawo kwadingeka ukuba ayozihlanganisa noNzwakele wakwaDube. Wathi ngoba nakhu sebebuya beyidlanzana wakha umuzi wawubiza ngokuthi kuseMandlanzini. Kusukela lapho kwavela isizwe saseMandlanzini.

AbakwaKhumalo nabakwaMabaso 
Izibongo zakwaKhumalo noMabaso, zivela emagameni amadodana kaMntungwa kaMbulazi. Laba bantu bangaMantungwa Nguni njengabantu bakwaZulu kanye nabakwaQwabe nabanye. 
Ukudabuka kwabo 
Kuthiwa badabuke eNingizimu neNtilasifali ngasoThaka. Ukudabuka kwabo kuyefana nokudabuka koMalandela kanye nabanye. 
  Ngingasho nje ukuthi phela yilapho ouke aMantungwa Nguni edabuka khona, asehla njalo ezongena kuleli eselaziwa ngokuthi kukwaZulu manje. AbakwaKhumalo kanye nabakwaMabaso base beholwa nguKhumalo kanye noMabaso. Ekusukeni kwabo enhla nezwe bafike bazinza endaweni yaseNquthu kusuka eMvunyane; Nondweni kuze kuyofika eMzinyathi. Kwathi abakWaMabaso bayokwenabela eNkandla koMa tshensikazi.

bakwaKhumalo kwakunguMagugu indodana 	kaGasa 
owayenomuzi wakhe waseSikhabeni. Waqale wakba eBabanango, kodwa ngokuhamba kwesikhathi wabuyela kwelaseNquthu. UMagugu nabantu bakwaKhumalo bakba ezintabeni zaseBabanango kuhambe njalo kuze kuyofika eNondweni. Babakbelene nabakwaKhoza kanye nabaseMachunwini, abaseZibisini kanye nabaseMancubeni. Kwabuye kwaba noqhekeko phakathi kwamadodana kaGasa oMagugu inkosana kanye nabanawakbe oDonda kanye noSiwela. 
  Bamshiya uMagugu bahamba noyisomncane uMashobana kanye nendodana kaMagawozi (uDloko) uBheje. Bahamba njalo baze bayofika ngaphesheya komfula iSikhwebezi. lapho uDonda wafike wakba umuzi wakbe awubiza ngokuthi kuSezizibeni. Ngalokbo wabizwa ngokuthi unguDonda weZiziba. Kwathi uBheje yena wakba umuzi wakhe eNgome owaziwa ngokuthi kuseTsheni likaBheje. USiwela kabange esafika yena kulolu fuduko, kodwa yindodana yakhe eyafika uMlotsha, yakba umuzi wayo waSothulini eduze kwegquma Amaphondwana. Kwathi uMashobana yena wayokwakba umuzi wakbe endaweni kusukelaeSikhwebezi kuze kuyoshaya eMkhuze. UMagugu wahlala eNquthu waze wahlaselwa nguShaka. 
  Kodwa kuze kube manje abantu bakwaKhumalo abayinzalo kaMagugu bagcwele eNtinini ngaseBabanango, eDriefontein eMnambithi kanye naseTilehe (Utrecht). Umasibuyela

    IUZIBHEBHU 
  Kuthe uNgoza uma ehlangana nobunzima emaMpondweni wasuka walibangisa ngaseNtshonalanga yezwe, eqonde kwelamaHiligwa, uNdabankulu yena wabuyela emuva ezweni lakubo eMhlumayo. Kodwa kuthe uma efika kbona wafica uShaka esebeke uJobe indodana kaMaphitha wakwaSithole, njengombheki waleya ndawo. eyibhekele uShaka uqobo. Wasuka wayokwakha phakathi kwemifula emibili uMtshezi kanye neMpofana. Okwathi ngelinye ilanga waphaphama 
130 



80. 
kuMantungwa afudukayo, sithola ukuthi noma uDonda wayeyinkosana kodwa umuntu owagqama kakhulu kwaba yindodana kaMashobana uMzilikazi. 
  UDonda wahlala nabantu bakhe baseZizibeni ngaphesheya kweSikhwebezi kwaze kwafika isikhathi lapho aze ahlaselwa khona nguZwide ngoba ethi uvuse inyamazane yakhe uShaka ayeyilungisele ugibe lokuba ibhajwe khona kodwa uDonda wayiphunyula. Indaba isuka ngoDingiswayo owabulawa nguZwide eyinkosi enkulu yakwaMthethwa. Kwathi ukuba uZwide amnqobe uDingiswayo ngobuqili bakhe, wase efuna ukubulala uShaka. Bathi-ke uZwide wayenezintelezi ezimbi ayezichela emngceleni wezwe lakhe. 
  Bathi kwakuthi uma isitha sakhe sike sazeqa lezi zintelezi. sasihungeka siphuphutheke size siyozithela ezandleni zamabutho kaZwide. NoDingiswayo walimala kanjalo. Nango phela ekuweleni iMfolozi ngakwaMpukunyoni, wahungeka wahamba nenduna yakhe eshiya amabutho akhe waze wayozithela emabuthweni kaZwide ayemlinde koMbuzi.' NoShaka, wayezobanjwa kalula kanjalo ngesikhathi ephuma kubo kwaZulu ekade eyokhalela uyise uSenzangakhona owayekhotheme ngalezo zinsuku. Ngesikhathi uShaka ebuya uDonda wamzwela, wafuna isu lokumsiza. Phela kwakukhona ukuzwana phakathi kukaDonda noDingiswayo. Ngakho ukufa kwakhe kwakumphethe kabi uDonda. 
  Kwathi ukuba ezwe ukuthi uShaka useyabuya kwaZulu, futhi uthukuthele ufuna ukuphindisela uDingiswayo kuZwide, uDonda wafisa ukumexwayisa. Ngenhlanhla indlela kaShaka yayizokwedlula ngalapho uDonda ekanise khona. Kwathi uShaka esesesikhaleni saMayiwane ngaseMhlabathini, wamhlangabeza uDonda wamkhalela ngezindaba ezibuhlungu. 
  Ekhalela uShaka ngokufelwa kwakhe ngoyise bobabili ngesikhathi esisodwa, ikakhulukazi uDingiswayo owayemkhulisile. Wase ernxwayisa ukuthi angalingi angene ezweni lakwaNdwandwe ngoba naye uyophenduka isithingithingi. UZwide ambambe ambulale ikhanda lakhe liyohlobisa kwaNtombazi. unina kaZwide. Nangempela uShaka wakulalela ukuxwayiswa yinsizwa endala, waphindela kubo 
132 
kwaNobamba, inhliziyo yakhe igaya izibozi efuna ukuziphindisela kuZwide, ngokubulala uyise ayemthanda ngaphezu kukayise omzalayo. 
  Zambikela uZwide izinhloli zakhe. Wathukuthela wagana unwabu. UZwide wayaziwa ngobuqili bakhe. Akathandanga ukumkhombisa uDonda ukuthi kumthukuthelisile ukwenza kwakhe. Uthe esuka uZwide wayefuna ukwenza obukhulu ubudlelwane noDonda. UDonda wakwazi ukuphephisa uShaka ebuqilini . bukaZwide kodwa wehluleka yena ukuba aziphephise. UZwide wacela uDonda ukuba ke bakhiphe ngokuhlanganyela inqina yomsenge, bese kuthi emva kwalokho kuba khona ijadu lapho kuzosina khona izintombi kuze kushone ilanga. 
  Usethi kuDonda angexwayi uma eza namabutho akhe ehlomile ngoba uyedlula usavakashela uShaka. Ngakho emva kwejadu uzobe esedlula. Nangempela uDonda nabantu bakhe bakholwa yile nsumansumane kaZwide. Kwathi ngalolo suku uZwide wabulala uDonda kanye nendodana yakhe yokuqala kwasinda enye yamadodana akhe uMaqandela, eyathi gala yephuka, nyawo zami ngibelethe. 
  Akazange edlule uZwide namabutho akwaNdwandwe, kodwa waphindela emuva ezweni lakhe. Eqinisweni wayesewenzile umsebenzi wakhe, ngoba wayengaqonde khona kuShaka kodwa inyamazane yakhe kwakunguDonda. Kuthe esefuna ukubulala uBheje, uMashobana wamvusa uBheje wamtshela ukuthi kabaleke. Nangempela wasinda uBheje kanjalo. Kepha uMashobana kasindanga ngoba uZwide wabhodlela kuye wambulala, ngoba ethi wethuse inyamazane yakhe. 
UMzilikazi 
.') 
Ngesikhathi uMashobana akha ngaphezu koMkhuze, waganwa inkosazana kaZwide egama layo kwakunguNompethu. UNompethu nguyena ozala iqhawe laMantungwa, elaziwa ngokuthi nguMzilikazi. Igama elithi Mzilikazi abanye balichaza ngezindlela eziningi. Abanye bathi nguMzila wegazi, abanye

81. 
ambulale uDonda nendodana yakhe wayesethi uMzilikazi kahambe 
bathi lisho umzila omkhulu. Kodwa sizothatha njengoba ayebizwa kasinakusho okunye futhi. Njengoba sishilo sathi uMzilikazi uzalwa nguMashobana kuNompethu, indodakazi kaZwide inkosi yakwaNdwandwe. 
  Lokho okusho ukuthi wayenegazi eligobhoza emithanjeni yakhe lasebukhosini bakwaNdwandwe nobakwaKhumalo ngoba phela uyise uMashobana wayephethe abantu bakwaKhumalo futhi noma uDonda wayengowasendlunkulu kodwa uMashobana nguyena owayenezwi eMantungweni onke ngoba nguyena owayenguyise wabo. Kanti futhi ukufa kukaMashobana noDonda kwenza ukuba abantu bakwaKhumalo babumbane kakhulu kunakuqala. 
  UMzilikazi njengoba wayezalwa yinkosazana kaZwide owayebusa isizwe esikhulu sakwaNdwandwe, kwafanela ukuba ayokhulela khona kwaNdwandwe ngaphansi kweso likayisemkhulu. Afunde futhi nokuba yibutho .kanye nobuqhawe kwizihlabani zakwaNdwandwe. Ngakho unpilo yakhe yonke yobunsizwa wayichitha kwaNdwandwe, esemabuthweni akwaNdwandwe. UZwide ubulala uDonda nendodana yakhe aze abulale noMashobane, uMzilikazi ukhona laphaya kwaNdwandwe, uyakubuka konke lokhu kwenzeka kubantu bakubo. Uyayibona ingwenya iqhobozela abantu bakubo. 
  Noma inhliziyo yayifutha kodwa wakufaka esiqundwini lokho elindele ukuthi liyoze lifike eliyisithutha. aziphindiselele kumkhulu wakhe obulale abantu bakubo ebansucula amakhanda ngaphandle kwesizathu. Sishilo phela sathi uMashobana wabulawela ukuthi uvuse uBheje wathi kabaleke ngoba nangu uZwide efuna ukumbulala. Sizwa ukuthi noNtombazi unina kaZwide akakujabulelanga ukubulawa komkhwenyana wornzukulu wakhe uNompethu. 
Bathi waze washo wathi lell khanda lizobabangela amashwa. 
Okwashiwo nguNtombazi kwafana nesipholofetho, ngoba kwenzeka kanjalo, njengoba wayeyitshelile indodana yakhe uZwide. 
  Kuthe ukuba uZwide kanye noMashobana, 
134 
ayophatha abantu bakwaKhumalo. Eqinisweni kwasakhona ukubusa kodwa uMzilikazi wayeseyophathela uZwide ngoba phela wayeseyinqobile indlu kaMntungwa futhi enethemba elikhulu lokuthi njengoba sekuyophatha uMzilikazi njengomzukulu wakhe, zonke izinto zizomhambela kahle ababuse kahle abantu bakwaKhumalo. 
  Kodwa akubanga njalo. Ngoba kuMzilikazi kwakufana nenhlamba lokhu ukuba uZwide athi akayomphathela abantu bakwaKhumalo kodwa ebebulele amakhosi akhona ikakhulukazi ebulele noyise. Wacabanga ukuthi abantu bakwaKhumalo uzobabheka kanjani? Abazukusho yini ukuthi usedayise ngabo kuZwide uyisemkhulu? Uthando lwabantu bakwaKhumalo kuMzilikazi lwakhula ngamandla kangangokuthi kwakhula enkulu inzondo yokuzonda lesi silwane esingumkhulu wakhe. Kwafika ukuthi kufanele abaphindisele abantu bakubo ngandlela thize. Ukuvuma kwakhe ukuba ayophatha abantu bakwaKhumalo eNgome, kwakungukuba ayothola kahle isu lokuthi angalakha kanjani isu lakhe ngenkulu impumelelo? Futhi wayefuna ukuba leli tulo alithunge ekanye nazo zonke izikhulu zakwaKhumalo ezazithukuthele zifile, zithuthumela ngento eyenziwe nguZwide. 
  Nokuthi nje akhombise abantu bakwaKhumalo ukuthi uzwelana nabo kwisehlo esibehlele, sidalwe nguyisemkhulu. Ekusukeni kwakhe uMzilikazi kwaNdwandwe, wakha umuzi wakhe ngasemthonjeni weSikhwebezi. Endaweni eyayinenqaba e!ihlekile, eyayaziwa ngabakwaKhumalo bodwa, eyayaziwa ngokuthi kuseNtubeni.

UMagawozi vena uzale uBheje vena ozale uMqhethi. 
Engingakuphawula lapha ukuthi abantu bakaSiwela yilaba asebezibiza ngokuthi abakwaNkosi Ndlangamandla. 
AbakwaNtshangase (Emgazini) 
Abantu bakwaNtshangase kanye nabakwaBiyela bavela emzini wenkosi uNdaba indodana kaMageba kaZulu kaMalandela. UNdaba wayenemizi yakhe, kodwa ngemibili engizoyibalula lapha. Owokuqala kuseMqekwini. Lona kwakuyiwona muzi omkhulu. Yilapho kwavela khona inkosi uJama nabafowabo oNkwelo noMhana ababebalulekile embusweni wakhe uJama. Umuzi wesibili kwakuseGazini. Ukuze kuthiwe kuseGazini kulo muzi yingoba yiwona muzi okwakuthi uma kunemicimbi yakomkhulu kuhlatshelwe khona. Ngakho kwakungumuzi obaluleke kakhulu esizweni sonke senkosi uNdaba. Lapha eMqekwini kwakukhona uShwankeni umfowabo kaXhoko kanye noMgutshwa nabanye. 
  Kwavela esikhulu isigemegeme ngesikhathi abantwana baseMqekwini sebefuna ukuganwa ngabantwana baseGazini. Abakuthandanga abaseGazini lokhu ngoba beth! laba ngabafowabo. Ngenxa yokuphikelela kwalaba baseMqekwini laba baseGazini baze bashintsha kungentando yabo kwase kuthiwa bangabaseMgazini. Kwaqhutshekwa nokuganana kwezingane, kodwa abaseMgazini noma sebebizwa kanjalo abakubusisanga lokhu kuganana. UXhoko kanye nabanye abafowabo bazama ukuba babiyele umuzi wabo ukuze kungenzeki lokhu abangakufuni. Base bebhinqwa kuthiwa babiyela umuzi. base bethola isibongo sokuthi ngabakwaBiyeia. Kwathi uShwankeni vena wathola esakwaNtshangase, ngoba kuthiwa bantshingiwe. Kunamaqhawe abalulekile kwaNtshangase afana noMdlaka owayeyinduna kaShaka kanye noMasiphula owayeyinduna kaMpande.

AbakwaMyeni 
Abantu bakwaMyeni bangamaNtungwa Nguni ngoba sengathi bahlobene kakhulu nabantu bakwaMabaso kanye nabaseMachunwini. Lokhu sikusho ngoba isizinda sabo silaphaya eBabanango eduze nomfula uMhlathuze. Lapho okwakuxhumeke khona uMabaso noMchunu. Ngesikhathi belaphaya eBabanango kwakungashiwo ukuthi ngabakwaMyeni, kodwa kwakuthiwa ngabakwaMyeki. Umuntu owayeyikhanda lalaba bantu kwakunguMlambo. Kwathi ngesikhathi sikaMlambo kwaba khona umbango emndenini lokho okwenza ukuthi uMlambo ashiye emanxiweni akubo ayozinza kwesenkosi yakwaQwabe. Wakha ngaseShowe, lapho uMlambo akhothamela khona. Ekufeni kukaMlambo washiya amadodana amabili uNgwenya inkosana kanye noNsinde omncane. UNgwenya wazala abakwaNgwenya kwathi uNsinde wazala abakwaNsinde. 
  Kwathi ngesikhathi sikaOuma indodana kaNgwenya. kwehla umhlolo ongakaze ubonwe kuleli likaMthaniya, lapho kwangena khona insingizi yakhala egcekeni. Lokhu kwakubika umhlola uqobo. 
  UOuma kalinda ukuba kuyiwe ohlanyeni kube nengomboco kodwa wavele waqoqa abantu bakayise abangakuye washaya wachitha wayokhonza enkosini yabaThembu eNseleni. Kuthe ukuba atholwe lapho wase eshintsha isibongo sakhe wathi sebengabakwaMyeni hhayi uMyeki. Lokhu kwamenza ehlukane nabafowabo ababesele kwaQwabe. 
Uzibiza ngoMyeni ngoba ethi sesingabayeni ezizweni. 
Kwakusengathi laba bantu base beqalile ukulunywa unyawo. Ngoba kabahlalanga futhi ebaJhenjini kodwa bedlula baze bayokwakha endaweni yakwaMlhethwa. bedlula futhi nalapho baze bayofinyelela eMatubatuba, sebewele iMfolozi emhlophe. Kwathi bethi bayazinza lapho base behlaselwa nguSoshangane wakwaNxumalo, wabadudula baze beqa izintaba zoBombo baye bafinyelela emfuleni iNgwavuma. Kulapho bahlangana

khona nabakwaMngomezulu okuyibona babephethe kuleya ndawo. 
  Bafike bemukeleka ngezandla ezimhlophe ngabantu bakwaMngomezulu. Inkosi yabo kwakunguZondiwe. Bahlala kahle abantu bakwaMyeni kule ndawo. Kuthiwa nendlu kaNsinde nayo yalandela abafowabo. 
  Kuthiwa abantu bakwaMngomezulu ngenxa yokulunga kwabo behlalisene ngokuthula nabantu bokuhamba, lokho kwabadalela enkulu inkinga ngoba bazibona sebefukamele inqwaba yabantu ababebalekela ulaka lukaShaka kangangokuba base behluleka ukubafukamela. 
  Lokho kwenza uZondiwe inkosi yakwaMngomezulu agudluke yena egudlukela laba bantu, ngoba ebona ukuthi bamdonsela amanzi ngomsele ngoba bathi babalekela ulaka lukaShaka. Washiya abanye babantu bakhe ezandleni zomfowabo uMsuduka. Bathi uZondiwe wafela kwabezizwe. 
Ukwelamana kwabakwaMyeni 
yakwaMyeni eyayisiyakhe eNtshaneni ezintabeni zoBombo, indodana kaYuma uSiphike, wasuka washiya izwe lakubo wayokwakha eSwazini, lapho afela khona kanye nendodana yakhe uMkakwa. Kepha uMlangazi kaLundini wahola isizwe sakwaMyeni ezintabeni zoBombo.

AmaMbatha 
Abantu baseMaMbatheni uma ubabuza ngemvelaphi yabo uthola izimpendulo ezahlukene. Abanye bathi baqhamuka ezweni labeSuthu belandela izintethe, abanye bathi baqhamuka ePutukezi. Uma ubuza ngesibongo sabo sokuthi Mbatha basho okunye okungakholakali. Esingathi kudshe 
kube yiqiniso 	esilithola 	kwabanye 	baseMaMbatheni 
nasekuphenyeni 	okunzulu, 	sithola 	ukuthi abantu 
baseMambatheni ngesikhathi senkosi yakwaZulu uJama, babakhe laphaya eNhlazatshe bebuswa nguShandu indodana kaNdaba. 
  Sizwa futhi ukuthi kukula makhosi omabili lapho kwavela khona ukuthi abantu bakaShandu babizwe ngokuthi ngabaseMaMbatheni. Kanti. abanye bathi kwathi ngesikhathi uShaka eyohiasela aMantungwa akwaSokhumalo, wedlula wathi uzobuya azohlasela aMaMbatha, kodwa kuthiwa aMaMbatha azincengela kuShaka aze abeka izingalo emahlombe. 
  Kwase kuthi ngokwenza kwabo wathi uShaka kabayekwe ngoba seze bembatha imikhono. Kwase kuthiwa ngaMaMbatha. Kodwa lokhu sikuthola kuphikisana nomlando, ngoba sithola emlandweni ukuthi ngesikhathi sikaShaka, uShandu wayengasekho sekukudala akhothama, kwase kubusa umzukulu wakhe uMancengeza indodana kaKhali kaShandu. Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi impi kaShaka noMancengeza yayiseMhlahlane. Wehlulwa uMancengeza wabaleka nabantu bakhe bayobhaca enqabeni yabo entabeni iNhlazatshe, kwathi abantu bakaMbudiele umfowabo kaKhali bona basheshe bazinikela kuShaka engakabathinti, kwathi abakaNkomo babalekela eDumbe noma babuye babuya bafike bazinza kumngani kaNkomo uNyanya wakwaDlamini eZihlalo.

  Ngakho iqiniso okucishe kube yilo ngelokuthi isibongo sikaMbatha savela ngesikhathi sikaJama ukhokho kaShaka noShandu ukhokho kaMancengeza. Kuthiwa indaba yasuswa yisithakazelo esithi Ndabezitha. Ngokwempela, isithakazelo esithi Ndabezitha ngesabantu bakaShandu ngoba sisuselwa emagameni okhokho babantu bakaShandu, okungoMpangazitha kanye noNdaba. Abantu babethophana ngokuthi Ndaba kaMpangazitha, Ndaba kaZitha. 
  Kwase kuvela uNdabezitha, ngenxa yolimi IwesiNtungwa lokugwinya amagama. UJama ngaphesheya komfula iMfolozi emhlophe wayekhathazekile ngesithakazelo sabo sokuthi bangabakwaLufenu lwenja. Wakubona kunganambitheki ukuthi intombazana yakwaZulu ithakazelwe ngale ndlela. Wakubona kungamahloni lokhu. Wasehahela isithakazelo sabantu bangaphesheya. Wafuna isu lokusithola lesi sithakazelo. 
  UJama wayemeya uShandu noma wayemazi ukuthi uhlakaniphile kodwa ngenxa yobufishane nobuncane bakhe kwenza uJama ameye kakhulu. Nakhu phela kuthiwa uShandu kangakanani nasentendeni yesandla uyalingana. Ngale uJama wayaziwa ukuthi uyakwazi ukuciba ngomkhonto. Wasebenzisa lell thuba-ke uJama, lokuba acele inselelo kuShandu, yokuba bayociba utholumbe. Uthi uma elwethula udaba kuShandu, uthi Nkosi Shandu kuthiwa ungumpetha ekucibeni, ngakho-ke kufanele kubonakale namhlanje ukuthi ngubani ongcono kunomunye. Sizociba kodwa into esizobekelana ngayo ukuthi oyophumelela uzothola umklomelo okuyisithakazelo esithi Ndabezitha. Kwaqala uShandu waciba, ngeshwa akaphumelelanga. UJama esikhundleni sokuba acibe into eyayibekiwe ukuba icitshwe, uJama wathatha umkhonto wakhe wathi uwuvalela esifubeni kuShandu kanti uShandu ubese"ekubone kudala okuhloswe nguJama. Wawuvika umkhonto ngokwembatha isiphuku, wawuphebeza ngaso ewuvika. Wayesethi uJama 'Ya! Wena wembatha isiphuku kusukela manje akuseyikushiwo kuwe kuthiwe Ndabezitha kodwa sekuzothiwa Mbatha. Satholakala kanjalo-ke isibongo saseMaMbatheni.

92. 
  Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi uNdaba uyise kaShandu wayezale amadodana amathathu, endala . kunguMbeje, ephakathi kunguShandu encane kunguDladla, kodwa ubukhosi bathathwa nguShandu ngoba engowasendlunkulu. 
  Uma sesibhekisisa kulolu hla lozalo IwaseMaMbatheni sithola ukuthi ubukhosi bagcina sebuwele endodaneni encane kaShandu uNkomo, ngoba uMancengeza ekwehlulweni nguShaka wabaleka nabantu bakhe bayozihlanganisa naBathembu bakaNgoza, eMsinga. Onke amaMbatha alaphaya eMsinga ngakaMancengeza kaKhali. Ezinye izindlu zikaShandu zesabela kude kwaze kwathi uHlakanyana kaMatshana, kaNkomo, waba yinceku eyethembekile kuMpande kangangokuthi waze wamganisela omunye wodadewabo. Wase ebuya eqoqa abantu bakwaMbatha, wase eba yinhloko yabo 
ngaphansi kweso likaMpande. 
Amaqhawe aseMaMbatheni sikhumbula uSimukanaye 
owafela Ondini Olumahlikihlikana ngesikhathi uZibhebhu ebulala izikhulu zasOndini. Siphinde sikhumbule uManyosi insizwa yaseZihlalo umfokaDlekezela, kaMpukane, kaNgwenya kaMashibha, kaShandu owayedume ngamahlaya akhe, kwaze kwavela nesisho sesiZulu esithi siyobohla Manyosi, ebhinqwa nguDingane ngoba esemhlamukile. Yena wakubonga lokho ngoba ethe indo dana yakhe ngokuthi nguSiyobohla. 
AmaMbatha bawehlukanisa kabili ngezindlu zawo. Kukhona amhlophe bese kuba khona amnyama. AmaMbatha ouke kaMngunyana nomfowabo uMandlovu babizwa ngokuthi ngaMaMbatha amhlophe, kanti abakaKhali, Mbudlele, Nkomo kanye nabakaMashibha baziwa njengaMaMbatha amnyama. UNkomo indodana encane kaShandu eyake yayozinza eDumbe yabulawa nguDingiswayo inkosi yakwaMthethwa, ikhiphela isibhongo kuyena ngoba ehlulekile ukuthola uKhali ayemqondile. Kwathi uMancengeza yena wahlaselwa nguShaka, yikho nje kuthiwa ezibongweni zikaShaka "Inkomo ekhale emthonjaneni, izizwe zonke ziyizwile ukulila ngoba izwiwe nguDunjwa wasOyengweni yezwiwa nguMancengeza 
kaKhali."

AbakwaMngomezulu 
Abantu bakwaMngomezulu, ngemvelaphi bayazalana nabakwaMathenjwa. Lokhu kusho ukuthi nabo badabuka ebeSuthwini babaPedi. Kutholakala ukuthi nomsunguli walesi sizwe wafela khona kwelabaPedi. Kususelwa kuyena ukuthi lesi sizwe sibizwe ngokuthi ngesakwaMngomezulu, ngoba igama lakhe kwakunguMngomezulu. 
  Kuthiwa indodana yakhe uMdluli wabona ukuthi kungcono afuduke ashone ngasolwandle, ayofuna amadlelo aluhlaza ayecabanga ukuthi uyohlangana nawo, kodwa akubanga njalo. Kodwa wahlangana nezinye izinkinga. 
	Bathi 	wehla 	njalo 	waze 	wakhwela 	ezintabeni 
zaseNgwavuma, lapho aze afela khona phezu komfula iNgwavuma ngasendaweni ebizwa ngokuthi kukwaNtshingila. Ekufeni kwakhe uMdluli washiya indodana yakhe uMafu. Kuthiwa uMafu wathanda ukufeza isifiso sabantu bakubo sokuba bayofika ogwini lolwandle. 
Wasuka wehla ezintabeni zoBombo waya eNtshaneni. 
Kodwa indlela yakhe kayithelanga ngoba ayekufuna akakutholanga, ngakho wabuyela khona eNgwavuma. Kuthiwa uMafu nabantu bakhe bagudla umfula iNgwavuma ngaphambi kokuba bazinze. Kuthiwa baze bahlangana nabantu bakwaThabede, nabo beziqhamukela eSwazini. Laba bantu bakwaThabede babezizingelela izindlovu. Bahlangana nabo 
156 
bakha ubuhlobo nabo, baganana. Kungaso leso sikhathi futhi lapho kwafika khona abantu bakwaMyeni. Ngesikhathi sokufika kwabakwaMyeni, abakwaMngomezulu base bebuswa nguZondiwe indodana kaDlakadla. 
  Kuthiwa abantu bakwaMngomezulu, noma babezihlalele ngokuthula kodwa lokho kuthula kwabo kwabadonsela izivakashi ezifika zifune ukukhoseliswa ngoba zibalekela izitha zazo. Phela kungaleso sikhathi lapho uShaka wayeshakazisa izwe. OSoshangane wakwaNxumalo kanye noZwangendaba wakwaPhakathi bedlula khona lapha kwelakwaMngomezulu bebalekela uShaka. Okubi okwakwenziwa ngabantu bakaZondiwe, ukuthi ngesikhathi laba bantu ababedlula endaweni yakwaMngomezulu behluphekile, bebaleka, uZondiwe wayezicebisa ngalaba bantu ngokuntshontsha imfuyo yabo. 
  UZondiwe wabuye wasuka walibangisa endaweni ebizwa ngokuthi kuseNkomazana okungumfula osenhla nezwe. Okwadabukisa ukuthi abantu bakwaMngomezulu kabazange bayilandele inkosi yabo, kodwa basala bona nomfowabo kaZondiwe uMsuduka. Kuthiwa wafike washona ekuhambeni uZondiwe washiya engenandodana eyothatha ubukhosi emva kwakhe. 
engakhiwe 	muntu 	basuka 	endaweni 	yakwaHlabisa 
bayokwakha kuleyo ndawo eyayixhumene nomfula uSuthu. 
  Sengathi ukusuka kwabantu bakwaMathenjwa endaweni lapho uMpande ayebabeke khona kwabadalela uhlevane kuMpande ngoba wabahlasela. Babaleka baze beqa uSuthu bayokwakha endaweni iJkwase kungeyamaPutukezi ngaleso sikhathi. Kwaze kwathi sekuphethe amaNgisi kulo lonke leli likaMthaniya, babuya abantu bakwaMathenjwa bazokwakha endaweni yabo yaseManyiseni. Ngesikhathi bebuyela ezweni labo abahlezi kulo kuze kube manje babeholwa nguMtshelekwana kaGamula.

93. 
  Kwasuka uMsuduka wangena omunye wamakhosikazi omfowabo, wathola umfana wabizwa ngokuthi nguLubelo. Okuthe uma esekhulile wase ethathil ubukhosi bakwaMngomezulu. Bathi into yokuqala nje ayenza uLubelo kwaba ukuhlasela abantu bakwaMyeni wabaxosha endaweni. Waxosha uMdolomba waze wayokhonza kuMpande kwaZulu. Akagcinanga ngokuhlasela abakwaMyeni wabuye wahlasela abakwaMathenjwa. Kodwa naye bagcina bembonile abanamehlo, ngoba uNtini. inkosi yakwaGumbi ihlangene nensalela yakwaMathenjwa kanye nabakwaNyawo bamhlasela wabaleka waze wayofika eSwazini, nakhona wafike wazithela kumalunda ngoba wafica inkosi yaseSwazini uMswati imlindele. Wabulawa esehamba nomlungu ethi uzomphephisa, kodwa lutho. Abantu bakhe babaleka babuyela ekhaya. 
AbakwaNyawo 
Abantu bakwaNyawo bangamaNtungwa Nguni, kabafani nabantu bakwaMathenjwa nabakwaMngomezulu, bona abavela ebaSuthwini. Abantu bakwaNyawo bafana nabantu bakwaMyeni. Okwenza ukuthi abantu bakwaNyawo kube sengathi bangamaSwazi ukuba basuke bayokwakha emngceleni wamaSwazi lena ngakwaHiathikhulu lapho kugcwele khona amathuna amakhosi akhona. Indawo lapho kutholakala khona abantu bakwaNyawo kusuka phakathi kwezintaba zoBombo ngasoPhongolo kuze kuyokuma ngomngcele welakwaMngomezulu. Kuthiwa yisizwe esikukhonze kakhulu ukuthula noxolo. Kodwa babezitnisela ekuzivikeleni uma behlaselwa izitha. zabo. Njengoba ngike ngasho ngaphambilini, abantu bakwaNyawo babenendawo yabo yokulondoloza amakhosi abo. Kwakuyisizwe esasikukhonzile ukugcina amasiko aso. Ngenxa yokuthi lesi sizwe sasikukhonzile ukuthula, lokhu kufakazelwa ukuthi in kosi uDingane ngesikhathi ehlaseJwa nguMpande esizana namaNgisi wabalekela kubantu bakwaNyawo, eyocela ukukhoseliswa. Nakho phela waze wafela khona. Idlinza lakhe likhona lapho eKwaliweni (Gwaliweni).

AbakwaMaphumulo/Mseleku/Shinga 
Ngibahlanganisa esihlokweni esisodwa laba bantu benezibongo ezahlukene ngoba uma sihlola umlando wabo, sithola ukuthi uyefana. Ukudabuka kwabo kunye. Bonke futhi bangaMalala. Kuthiwa bengakagudluzwa yizimpi ezanyakazisa bonke abantu abangamaNguni babakhe laphaya ngaseMgungundlovana eduze komfula owaziwa ngokuthi yiHlimbithwa eduze nje koThukela. Abantu ababakhelene nabo kwakungabakwaHlongwa, nabo bengakagudluzwa izimpi, baya ngaseMkhomazi. 
  Kuthiwa abantu bakwaMaphumulo ibona abayindlenkulu, kulandele eyaseMaselekwini, lapho kuphuma khona eyakwaShinga. Kuthiwa laba bantu baseMaselekwini bangabakwaMaphumulo. Kodwa ukuze kube ngabantu baseMaselekwini yingoba kwathi kuhlasele impi bonke abantu bebaleka bona banele bafika osebeni lolwandle base bayakhohlwa ukuthi kuyabalekwa balibala ukuzidlela lokhu okwakubizwa ngokuthi ngamaseleku (okungamasenene ngolimi IwamaThonga). Umuntu owaba khona kwaMaphumulo, nguDibandlela, indodana kaLubheleni. Kwathi ngesikhathi uMpande ebalekela umfowabo uDingane wawela nabo abantu bakwaMaphumulo baze bayokwakha ezansi noMlazi, okwase kunguMashimane owayesebusa abantu bakwaMaphumulo ngaleso sikhathi. 
159 




94. 
  Okunye okubaiulekile kubantu bakwaMaphumulo yimithi ekhaliphile kaManembe kanye nezintelezi zakhe aqala ukuzisebenzisa kuMpande kwaze kwaba sendodaneni yakhe uCetshwayo. 
  Yizona phela izintelezi zikaManembe nendodana yakhe uPhambana ezenza uCetshwayo anqobe empini yakhe nomfowabo uMbuyazi eNdondakusuka. Okubuhlungu wukuthi uManembe wabuye wabulawa nguyena uCetshwayo, kasazi-ke ukuthi kwase kwenzenjani. kodwa kusengathi kwase kukhona uKhondlo wakwaMazibuko owayesenamandla kakhulu kunoManembe. 
  Abantu baseMaselekwini bona babuye behlukana phakathi kwaba khona abazibiza ngokuthi ngabakwaDuma abanye bazibiza ngokuthi ngabakwaShinga. Okwaba nomehluko omkhulu futhi kwamangaza ukubona abakwaDuma bona 
	bebambelele 	kakhulu 	kwabakwaMaphumulo, 
	kunabakwaShinga. 	AbakwaDuma 	baqoqana laphaya 
ngaseMzinto endaweni okuthiwa manje kukwaDumisa ngenxa yomnumzane wakwaDuma owayebizwa ngokuthi nguDumisa. Kulaba bantu bakwaDurnisa kuphuma abantu bakwaGininda, Bongwa kanye nabakwaNdokweni. 
AbakwaShinga 
Abantu bakwaShinga ababuye baba ngabantu bakwaNdelu, behlukana nabantu bakwaMaphumulo ngesikhathi bonke beshakaziswa izimpi zamakhosi akwaZulu. Bona kabalingisanga abantu bakubo eMaselekwini oDuma, abaqhubeka nokuxhumana ngobuhlobo nabakwaMaphumulo, bona baba yisizwe esizimele geqe. Kwathi abakwaShinga bezihlalele eLovu lapho base bakhe khona, kwafika impi kaShaka ivakashele amaMpondo, wedlula kubantu bakwaNdelu wabakhumbuza ukuthi ukhona kulo lonke izwe, akukho lapho engenakufika khona. Abantu bakwaShinga base bephethwe nguNovanywa kanye noNdelu. 
  Kulolo hlaselo wafa uNovanywa, kwasala uNdelu wafuduka naye nabantu bakhe baze bayokwakha eMthwalume. Kulaba bantu bakwaShinga kwakukhona indoda egama layo 
160 
kwakunguMvuzi eyayakhe eMvoti eyabusiswa ngamadodana amabili. La madodana kwakungoGcwensa kanye noMzilini abaveza ezinye izibongo ezincane, njengesakwaGcwensa nje.

AbakwaNzuza 
Abantu bakwaNzuza ngokusempeleni akusibona abakwaZulu, kodwa baqhamuka eLusuthu. Ukufika kwabo kwelakwaZulu bafika ngesikhathi amakhosi efuna izinyanga eziqinile zokuqinisa amabutho awo ukuze babe namabutho aqinile futhi banqobe kalula izimpi. 
  Kwenzeka-ke ukuthi indoda ethize eyayiqhamuka kwelabeSuthu, yayingumuntu owaziyo amakhambi lana ayefunwa ngamakhosi. 
  Yona yayihamba izifunela indawo yokwakha, kwamsiza-ke lokhu kwazi kwakhe amakhambi lana, ngoba kwamtholisa indawo yokwakha kwelakwaZulu. Kuthiwa kwakuyinkosi uSenzangakhona okwafika kuye indoda yoMsuthu egama layo kwakunguMgidi. owayehamba nendodana ayakhe uNondumo kanye nomnawakhe uMqalane bephuma esizweni sakwaMaboko, phakathi nezwe.

  Kuthiwa umuntu okunguyena owathola indawo kwaZulu kwaba nguNondumo indodana kaMgidi, owayinikwa nguShaka. UShaka wanika Ie ndoda indaw(') eseduze nomfula uMfule lapho kwakwakhe khona abakwaXulu. Laphaya eMfule, uNondumo wayithola leya ndawo ngoba ebeyinyanga yempi kaShaka eyayilwa noZwide kaLanga wakwaNdwandwe. UNondumo kuthe ukuba athole indawo lena wayesethi, sengithole indawo ngiyizuze ngemithi yami kwase kuthiwa bangabakwaNzuza ngoba bezuze izwe ngemithi noma ngokwelapha.

  Waze wanikwa indawo okufanele ayiphathe eyaba yisabelo sakhe eseduze koThukela iMpaphala kuze kuyoshaya eMfongosi.. Kwathi sekubusa uDingane, uNdlela wathola isikhundla esithe xaxa sokuba ngundunankulu wezernpi ngaphansi kukaDingane. Nizokhurnbula ukuthi baba negalelo elikhulu benoNzobo. wakwaNtornbela ekubulaweni kwarnaBhunu eMgungundlovu ngo-1838. Nguyena futhi uNdlela owasindisa uMpande ekubulaweni ngumfowabo uDingane. Ngesikhathi uDingane efuna ukubulala uMpande, uNdlela wakhuza wababaza ethi uDingane uzongcolisa izandla zakhe ngokubulala uMpande engaphilile, eziphathelwe ngumchoboka. UNdlela wafa ebulawa nguDingane embulalela uMpande emva kwempi yaseMaqongqo. 
elwela inkosi yakhe. Sizokhumbula ukuthi uGodide ulele laphaya Ondini Olumahlikihlikana, ebulawa yimpi kaZibhebhu eyayizobhubhisa inkosi uCetshwayo. 
  UGodide kaNdlela walela lapho kanye nezinye izikhulu zikaZulu ezifana noSekethwayo wakwaMdlalose ebaQulusini, phela bafa ngoMaquba (July) zingamashumi amabili nanye kunyaka wenkulungwane namakhulu ayisishiyagalombili, namashumi ayisishiyagalombili nantathu (2! July 1883).

AbakwaKhoza 
Urnlando wabantu bakwaKhoza nemvelaphi yabo iyefana neyabantu bakwaKhumalo, Mabaso kanye naBathembu, ngoba bonke \ baqhamuka noma ngithi badabuka ndawonye. Ngokomlando nemvelaphi yalaba bantu kuveza izinkomba zokuthi babenobuhlobo bezalana futhi. Noma sebefuduka bahamba ngomgudu owodwa, baze bayozinza endaweni eyodwa. Phela sithola ukuthi bonke bazinza ezinkalweni zaseNquthu, Babanango kanye naseNkandla. Yilapho isizwe sakwaKhoza sazinza khona. Kukhona abathi isizwe sakwaKhoza ngabeSuthu. Nalokho kungaba yiqiniso ngoba uma sizwa onke aMantungwa adabuka eNingizimu neNtilasifali, yingakho nje bethi ahlobene nabeSuthu. Kuthiwa abantu bakwaKhoza, kwakungabantu abathanda ukuthula. Ukuthula kwabo kwaze kwaqedwa izimpi zakwaZulu, ikakhulukazi izimpi zikaShaka.

indo dana yakhe isencane uMaqwebelende, kanjalo naye flithi walandela indlela kayise, ngoba wabulawa nguShaka esemncane, kwathi umnawakhe uNgoza wathathwa wasindiswa ukuthi wayesemncane. Ngakho wakhoseliswa nguLukhwazi wakwaNtombela. Wakhula lapho njengendodana yakhe. 'Kwaze kwathi esekhulile wangena ebuthweni leziNyosi. Kodwa kwakukhona USikhonyane, owayezalwa nguNgqungqulu umfowabo kaMbiwa, uyise kaMaqwebelende. 
	Waba 	ngumuntu 	obalulekile 	nogqamile 	kubantu 
ababeyimithonsela eyayisele yakwaKhoza. Kwathi uNgoza esekhulile kodwa esahlezi kwaLukhwazi, uSikhonyane waheha uNgoza ukuba abuye eze ekhaya, kanti umyengela ophathe. Ekufikeni kwakhe wabulawa .. Washiya indodana uMganu. USikhonyane wahlala nabakwaBiyela laphaya eShowe.

  Kwathi ngesikhathi kuxabene uDingane kanye noMpande, uSikhonyane welekelela uMpande. Ngakho-ke ngaphansi kombuso kaMpande wasikelwa indawo ukuba ayiphathe laphaya eShowe. Ekukhothameni kwakhe washiya indodana yakhe uMfokazi owaganwa yindodakazi kaMpande uPopoza. Kepha uPopoza katholanga mntwana ngakho kwathathwa
